9.5.2.22	abhiprayāyam abhiṣuṇvanti samānatrābhiṣuṇvanti
9.5.2.23	dīkṣodavasānaṃ vā
9.5.2.24	āgneya aindāgno vaiṣṇavaḥ pauṣṇo vāyavya āśvinaḥ ṣaḍ atiriktāḥ paśavaḥ sattreṣu
9.5.3.1	gavām ayanaṃ prajātikāmā upeyus tenādityānām ayanaṃ vyākhyātam aṅgirasāṃ ca
9.5.3.2	trivṛtpañcadaśastomaḥ ṣaḍahānāṃ purastāt pṛṣṭhyo māsānāṃ prāg viṣuvataḥ pañcadaśatrivṛd upariṣṭān madhye pṛṣṭhyo māsānām
9.5.3.3	bṛhaspatisave 'bhijitaḥ sthāne viśvajita indrastomas tasmād uttaraḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍahaś ca daśarātro vyūḍhā agniṣṭomās trivṛta udbhidbalabhidau ca / so 'ṣṭāviṃśatyahaḥ
9.5.3.4	pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho madhye goāyuṣī avarūḍhastomaś chandomadaśāhaḥ
9.5.3.5	gavām ayanena śeṣo vyākhyātaḥ svargakāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.6	aṅgirasām ayanaṃ trivṛtstomaḥ ṣaḍahānāṃ purastāt pṛṣṭhyo māsānāṃ prāg viṣuvata ūrdhvam upariṣṭāt pṛṣṭhyo māsānām
9.5.3.7	ṣaḍahayoś cāyuś ca gauś cānulomaś chandomadaśāhaḥ
9.5.3.8	ādityānām ayanena śeṣo vyākhyātaḥ / svargakāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.9	dṛtivātavator ayanaṃ pṛṣṭhyasyaikaikenāhnā prāg viṣuvato māsān yanti / viṣuvataḥ sthāne mahāvrataṃ tair evāvṛttair upariṣṭāt prathamottame ahanī sātirātre / ṛddhikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.10	kuṇḍapāyinām ayanaṃ māsaṃ dīkṣitā bhavanti / te māsi rājānaṃ krīṇanti
9.5.3.11	dvādaśopasada uttamāyām upasady āparāhṇikīṃ saṃsthāpya somaṃ mahāvīrāṃś ca nidhāyāgnihotreṇa darśapaurṇamāsābhyāṃ caturbhiś cāturmāsyaparvabhir ekaikena māsān yanti
9.5.3.12	ardhamāsaṃ paurṇamāsīm ardhamāsam amāvāsyāṃ saṃsthāpya śunāsīryam utsādya mahāvīrān agnipraṇayanaprabhṛti payodohanāntaṃ kṛtvā vasanti
9.5.3.13	śvobhūte prātaranuvākaprabhṛti pañcabhiḥ pṛṣṭhyāhobhir ekaikena māsān yanti
9.5.3.14	aṣṭādaśa trayastriṃśāny ahāni daśarātro mahāvratam udayanīyo 'tirātraḥ sa māsaḥ
9.5.3.15	atsarukaiś camasaiḥ somān bhakṣayanti
9.5.3.16	yo hotā sādhvaryuḥ sa potā ya udgātā so 'chāvākaḥ sa neṣṭā yo maitrāvaruṇaḥ sa brahmā sa pratihartā yaḥ prastotā sa brāhmaṇāchaṃsī sa grāvastud yaḥ pratiprasthātā so 'gnītsa unnetā / sa māsam adhīte / gṛhapatirgṛhapatiḥ subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyaḥ
9.5.3.17	na varuṇapraghāseṣv avabhṛthaṃ yanti / bhūtikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.18	kṣullakatāpaścitaṃ caturo māsān dīkṣitā bhavanti / catasṛbhir upasadbhiś caranti
9.5.3.19	caturbhiḥ pṛṣṭhyāhobhir ekaikena māsān yanti / svargakāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.20	madhyamatāpaścitaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ dīkṣitā bhavanti / saṃvatsaram upasadbhiś caranti
9.5.3.21	gavām ayanaṃ sutyā / prajātikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.22	gavām ayanam ādityānām ayanam aṅgirasāṃ ca triḥsaṃvatsaraṃ sutyā / prathamottame ahanī sātirātre / ṛddhikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.24	naimiṣīyāṇām ayanaṃ dvādaśasaṃvatsaraṃ tair evāhobhir ekaikena trīṃstrīn saṃvatsarān yanti / svargakāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.25	śāktyānām ayanaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśatsaṃvatsaraṃ tair evāhobhir ekaikena navanava saṃvatsarān yanti
9.5.3.26	tarasamayāḥ puroḍāśāḥ sutyāsu / mṛgapakṣiṇāṃ praśastānāṃ śukānāṃ māṃsānāṃ pṛṣṭhyapuroḍāśān kurvanti yathocitam ṛddhikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.27	sādhyānām ayanaṃ śatasaṃvatsaraṃ tair evāhobhir ekaikena pañcaviṃśatiṃpañcaviṃśatiṃ saṃvatsarān yanti / svargakāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.3.28	atirātrayor madhye sahasram ahāni śatakṛtvo daśarātrasya veti sahasrasāvyaṃ vi pāpmanā vartemahītikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.4.1	sarasvatyā apyaye dīkṣate
9.5.4.2	cakrīvanti dīkṣitasya śālāgnīdhrasadohavirdhānāni ca
9.5.4.3	vedimātre saṃmimīyur na vediṃ mimīte nottaravedim
9.5.4.4	ulūkhalabaddho yūpaḥ prakṛṣyaḥ
9.5.4.5	abhiṣuṇvanti noparavān khananti
9.5.4.6	atirātre savanīyasya vapāṃ hutvendrāya sāṃnāyyāya vatsān apākaroti
9.5.4.7	agniṣṭomaṃ saṃsthāpyedhmābarhiḥ saṃnahyati
9.5.4.8	ṣoḍaśinaṃ saṃsthāpya sāyaṃ dohayati
9.5.4.9	atirātraṃ saṃsthāpya sāṃnāyyena yajante
9.5.4.10	sāṃnāyyaṃ saṃsthāpyāgreṇāhavanīyam avasthāyādhvaryuḥ prācīṃ śamyāṃ prāsyati / sā yatra nipatati tad gārhapatyasthānaṃ tataḥ ṣaṭtriṃśatprakrameṣv āhavanīyaḥ
9.5.4.11	tatrānuparyāhṛtyāgnīdhravedimātre sadohavirdhānāni pratiṣṭhāpya sāṃnāyyena yajante / tena pūrvapakṣaṃ yanti
9.5.4.12	gaur ukthyaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ saṃsthite paurṇamāsena yajante / tenāparapakṣaṃ yanti
9.5.4.13	āyur ukthyo 'māvāsyāyām
9.5.4.14	sāṃnāyyena pūrvapakṣān yanti paurṇamāsenāparapakṣān
9.5.4.15	dīkṣiṣyamāṇāḥ śate goṣv ṛṣabham utsṛjanti
9.5.4.16	tā yatra sahasraṃ saṃpadyante tadutthānaṃ sarvāsūpahatāsūtthānaṃ gṛhapatau preta utthānaṃ plākṣaṃ prasravaṇaṃ prāpyotthānam
9.5.4.17	sahasre saṃpanne gaur udayanīyo 'tirātraḥ sarvāsūpahatāsu viśvajid gṛhapatau preta āyuḥ
9.5.4.18	yady arvāk plākṣāt prasravaṇād uttiṣṭheran sthalair madhyasyottarato hrade 'vabhṛtham abhyaveyuḥ
9.5.4.19	plākṣaṃ prasravaṇaṃ yanto dṛṣadvatyā apyaye nirvaped aponaptrīyaṃ carum
9.5.4.20	plākṣaṃ prasravaṇaṃ prāpya niṣadi nirupyam udayanīyam atirātraṃ saṃsthāpyāgnaye kāmāyāṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
9.5.4.21	tasyām aśvāṃ ca puruṣīṃ ca dhenuke dakṣiṇe dattvā kārapacavaṃ prati yamunām avabhṛtham abhyaveyuḥ
9.5.4.22	mitrāvaruṇayor ayanaṃ sārasvataṃ svargakāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.4.23	mitrāvaruṇayor ayanenendrāgnyor ayanaṃ vyākhyātam aryamṇaś ca
9.5.4.24	trivṛtpañcadaśābhyāṃ vyatyāsam ardhayantīndrāgnyor ayane / tryaheṇatryaheṇābhyāvartayam aryamṇo 'yane 'bhijit paurṇamāsyāṃ viśvajid amāvāsyāyāṃ yathoktaṃ pūrvasmin
9.5.4.25	sarvāsāṃ prajānāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ syāmetikāmā upeyuḥ / pra devayānaṃ panthānam aśnavāmahā ity uttare
9.5.4.26	amāvāsyāyāṃ keśaśmaśrū yajamāno vāpayitvāplutyāhate kṣaume paridhāya paścād āhavanīyasyādīkṣitaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ pratimuñcati
9.5.4.27	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ pūrvāhṇe nirvaped aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālaṃ madhyaṃdine vaiśvadevaṃ carum aparāhṇe
9.5.4.28	tadbhakṣa etām eva trihaviṣam iṣṭiṃ nirvapet
9.5.4.29	tayā saṃvatsaraṃ yajeta
9.5.4.30	nānyat kṛṣṇājinād dīkṣitavratānāṃ kuryāt
9.5.4.31	samāpte saṃvatsare 'vabhṛthād udetya nikhilaṃ keśaśmaśrū yajamāno vāpayate
9.5.4.32	turāyaṇam ṛddhikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.4.33	saṃvatsaraṃ brāhmaṇasya gorakṣaḥ / saṃvatsaraṃ vyarṇe naitandhave 'gnim indhaḥ
9.5.4.34	samāpte saṃvatsare pariṇahyagnīn ādhāya dṛṣadvatyā apyaye nirvaped āgneyam aṣṭākapālam
9.5.4.35	dṛṣadvatyā dakṣiṇena tīreṇa śamyāparāsīyāt triplakṣaṃ prāpya yamunām avabhṛtham abhyaveyāt
9.5.4.36	tad evā manuṣyebhyas tiro bhavati / svargakāmo dārṣadvatam upeyāt
9.5.4.37	atirātrayor madhye 'gniṣṭomāḥ / sarvo daśadaśī saṃvatsaro dvādaśo viṣuvān sarpasāmāni viṣuvati kriyante
9.5.4.38	jarvaro gṛhapatir dhṛtarāṣṭra airāvato brahmety evamādīn sarpān āyur vijaye 'dhīyate
9.5.4.39	sarpasattram ṛddhikāmā amṛtatvakāmāḥ svargakāmāś copeyuḥ
9.5.4.40	atirātrayor madhye sahasraṃ trivṛtaḥ saṃvatsarān daśarātraṃ vā saṃtatam ekaikaṃ saṃvatsaram etya prajāpater evaṃ sahasrasaṃvatsaraṃ prajātikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.4.41	caturbhiḥ pṛṣṭhyāhobhir ekaikena pañca pañcāśataṃ saṃvatsarān yanti
9.5.4.42	viśvasṛjām ayanaṃ sahasrasaṃvatsaraṃ sarvā naḥ prajā anuprajāyeran brahmalokaṃ ca gachemahītikāmā upeyuḥ
9.5.4.43	tatra śloko 'pyuktaḥ
9.5.4.43a	viśvasṛjaḥ prathame sattram āsata sahasrasavaṃ prasavena yantaḥ
9.5.4.43c	tato ha jajñe bhuvanasya goptā hiraṇmayaḥ śakuno brahmanāma
9.5.4.43	iti
9.5.4.44	sarasvatyūnāni kalpayatu kalpayatu
9.5.5.1	cāturhotṛkagonāmikam apy anāhitāgner dvādaśarātraṃ trirātram ekarātraṃ vā
9.5.5.2	pākayajñopacārād agnim upacarati
9.5.5.3	sāṃgrāmikī jayasya dakṣiṇā saptasthavīryeṣu vāso deyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ vā deyam
9.5.5.4	revatyāṃ citrāyāṃ vā paśukāmaḥ karma kurvīta
9.5.5.5	bhinnena sravatā na hastā avanenijīta na pibed ayaspātreṇety eke tad deśapratiṣedham ity apare
9.5.5.6	yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya gavāṃ madhye 'raṇye 'dhītair gonāmabhir āhvayet
9.5.5.7	saṃśṛṅgīṃ purastāt pratīcīm avasthāpyādhastād darbhān āstīrya kāmyāyai svāheti mūrdhani tisra āhutīḥ paśukāmo juhuyāt
9.5.5.8	uttaro nigade vyākhyātaḥ
9.5.5.10	prācīnapravaṇe samūle paśukāma upodaye sūryasya hastā avanijya darbhastamba udaśarāvaṃ ninayet kāmaṃkāmaṃ ma āvartayeti
9.5.5.11	gobhiḥ sahetya praśastāḥ stha kalyāṇya iti brūyāt
9.5.5.12	ekāṣṭakāyāṃ catuṣpathe 'ṅgaśo gāṃ kārayed yoya āgachet tasmaitasmai dadyāt
9.5.5.13	śvo 'nyāṃ kārayitvā brāhmaṇān bhojayet paśukāmaḥ
9.5.5.14	uttaro nigade vyākhyātaḥ
9.5.5.15	vasīyasy ehi śreyasy ehīti sapta devagavyaś cid asi manāsi dhīrasīty uttarāḥ sapta / tāsām anuprāṇāntāḥ prathamā ehyantā uttarāḥ
9.5.5.16	saha rāyaspoṣeṇa devīr devīr ity anunigadati
9.5.5.17	saṃgrāmaṃ jigīṣan senayoḥ saṃdṛśyamānayoḥ pūrvābhir hutvottarā nigadet
9.5.5.18	yatra samūlā oṣadhīr upagachet paśūn vā tad etā ehyantāḥ sapta japet
9.5.5.19	saptasthavīrye saptānāṃ gavām ājyaṃ saptānāṃ payasi sthālīpākaḥ
9.5.5.20	yasya sapta sthavirāś caramām antamā syuḥ pūrvābhir hutvottarā nigadet
9.5.5.21	yo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā bahupuṣṭaḥ syāt tasya gavāṃ sāṇḍaṃ vatsataram ilāndāḥ stha pūṣṇo nakṣatraṃ poṣayiṣṇv ity apagamayeta
9.5.5.22	āyur me dā iti svāsu goṣṭhāsv avasṛjya vasīyasy ehi śreyasy ehīti parasyātyāhvayet
9.5.5.23	sārasvataṃ payasi sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā sārasvata ṛgbhyām āhutīr juhuyād etena grāmakāmo yajeta tathā paśukāmaḥ
9.5.5.24	sarvāsāṃ dugdhe catuḥśarāvam odanaṃ paced brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paśukāmaḥ
9.5.5.25	na chinnaṃ deyam iti vyākhyātam
9.5.5.26	tāṃ bhadraṃbhadram iti brūyād bhadraṃ kalyāṇam iti brūyāt puṇyaṃ praśastam iti brūyāt
9.5.5.27	adīkṣaṇīyāya gāṃ dattvā na me tad upadambhiṣar dhṛṣir iti japet
9.5.6.1	vīravatīr bhūyāsta iti vyākhyātam ā balihṛtaḥ
9.5.6.2	bhūyāṃso bhūyāsta iti sabhāsadaḥ
9.5.6.3	pādau pratyavahared upopatiṣṭheta vā
9.5.6.4	puṇyā puṇyam asūd iti vyākhyātaṃ puṇyam asūd iti vā
9.5.6.5	ekāṣṭakāyāṃ tūṣṇīṃ sarvān saṃsṛjya puṇyāḥ puṇyān asuvaṃś citrāś citrān asuvann aiḍā me bhagavanto 'janiḍhvaṃ maitrāvaruṇa ūrjā me bhagavantaḥ sahājaniḍhvaṃ saṃvidaṃ me vindateti puṃso jātān puṇyāḥ puṇyā asuvaṃś citrāś citrā asuvann aiḍyo me bhagavatyo 'janiḍhvaṃ maitrāvaruṇyo rāyaspoṣeṇa me bhagavatyaḥ sahājaniḍhvaṃ jñātraṃ me vindateti strīr jātās tān ubhayān sahābhimantrayeta
9.5.6.6	dhenuṃdhenum iti brūyād dhenur bhavyeti brūyān na hateti brūyāt kuruteti brūyān nāntarvatnīti brūyād vijanyeti brūyāt
9.5.6.7	ikṣukāṇḍam apsu vāsayitvā lohitenāyasena vā
9.5.6.8	bhuvanam asi sāhasram indrāya tvā sṛmo 'dadād yāvatīnām idaṃ karomi bhūyasīnām uttarāṃ samāṃ kriyāsam iti gavāṃ lakṣma kuryāt ṣaṇṇāṃ catasṛṇāṃ vā / puṃsaḥ striya iti vyatyāsam
9.5.6.9	yasya dakṣiṇataḥ pratibhinnam iti vyākhyātam
9.5.6.10	iha prajā viśvarūpā ramantām iti gāḥ sāyam āyatīr abhimantrayeta
9.5.6.11	saṃ vaḥ sṛjatv aryameti gāḥ saṃsṛjed yā asya purā syur yāś cānyato vindeta
9.5.6.12	revatī tantir iti tantiṃ vitanuyāt prācīm udīcīṃ vā
9.5.6.13	dadhi ghṛtena saṃsṛjya rayyā tvā puṣṭyānumārjmīty anumārṣṭi
9.5.6.14	tasyāḥ pramuktavatsāyā vratāni na riktā syāt
9.5.6.15	noparyupari saṃcareyur nābhivarṣen nābhitapet
9.5.6.16	ṛṣabham utsrakṣyan pitā vatsānām ity ṛṣabhasya dakṣiṇe karṇe utsṛjamāno japet retodhāṃ tvā yaśodhāṃ rāyaspoṣāyotsṛja ity utsṛṣṭe
9.5.6.17	yo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā bahupuṣṭaḥ syāt tasya gavāṃ goṣṭhād ekaviṃśatiṃ śakāny āhṛtyaikaviṃśatim āhutīḥ paśukāmo juhuyāt
9.5.6.18	gonāmabhir devagavībhir ākṛtihomair agrato gāminīṃ paścāt pratīcīm avasthāpyādhastād darbhān āstīrya kāmyāyai svāheti bhasadi tisra āhutīḥ paśukāmo juhuyāt
9.5.6.19	yāsām indra udājateti catvāra ākṛtihomā etaiḥ pūrvāhṇe goṣṭhāsu goṣu juhuyād etair madhyāhne goṣv ākṛtāsv etair aparāhṇe goṣṭhāsu gatāsv etaiḥ saṃgrāme
9.5.6.20	mitrabhṛtaḥ kṣatrabhṛtaḥ ity aśvān abhimantrayate
9.5.6.21	rohiṇīr vo vṛñja iti saptājyasyāhutīḥ paśukāmo juhuyāt
9.5.6.22	paurṇamāsīm aṣṭakām amāvāsyāṃ citrām aśvatthaṃ na gām apākuryāt
9.5.6.23	govarcasaṃ guptasyeti sarpiṣa ubhayeṣāṃ tvā devamanuṣyāṇām iti vyākhyātaṃ priyaṃ karomīti śrotriyasya priyāṃ karomīti kumāryāḥ patikāmāyāś cāmuṣya cety avabhṛthe
9.5.6.24	uttaro nigade vyākhyātaḥ
9.5.6.25	annādyakāmaḥ śabalīkarma kuryāt
9.5.6.26	trayodaśyām udite yatra grāmasya paśoḥ śabdaṃ nopaśṛṇuyāt tad araṇyaṃ paretya brāhmaṇaṃ bahuvidam upaviśya darbhastambam ārabhya śabali śabaly ehīti trir āhvayet
9.5.6.27	yad anyac chuno gardabhād vā pratiśṛṇuyāt sā samiddhiḥ
9.5.6.28	yadi na pratiśṛṇuyāt saṃvatsare punar āhvayen na tṛtīyakam āhvayet
10.1.1.1	athātaḥ śulbaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
10.1.1.2	rajjuṃ pāśavatīṃ samāṃ nirāyatāṃ pṛṣṭhyāṃ yathārtham upakalpayet
10.1.1.3	antareṇa citrāsvātī śravaṇapratiśravaṇau kṛttikāpratikṛttike tiṣyapunarvasū ca prāgdeśo 'yaṃ yugamātroditayoḥ pāśāñ ca
10.1.1.4a	dārśikyāḥ śayāḥ ṣaṭtāni sapta saptadaśaiva tu
10.1.1.4c	ekaṃ dve pañca tair mītvā samaraiḥ parilekhayet
10.1.1.5	aṃsāc chroṇau rajjvantaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya prācīm anulikhed aṃse pratiṣṭhāpya pratīcīṃ samare rajjvantaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śroṇer adhy aṃsād anulikhet
10.1.1.6	evam uttarataḥ purastāt paścāc ca
10.1.1.7a	saratniś caturasras tu pūrvasyāgneḥ kharo bhavet
10.1.1.7c	rathacakrākṛtiḥ paścāc candrārdhena tu dakṣiṇe
10.1.1.8a	madhyāt koṭipramāṇena maṇḍalaṃ parilekhayet
10.1.1.8c	atiriktatribhāgena sarvaṃ tu sahamaṇḍalam
10.1.1.8a	caturasre 'kṣṇayā rajjur madhyataḥ saṃnipātayet
10.1.1.8c	parilekhyā tadardhenārdhamaṇḍalam eva tat
10.1.1.9	gārhapatyāhavanīyāv antarā rajjuṃ nimāyāparasmiṃs tṛtīye lakṣaṇaṃ madhyāt turīyam utsṛjya lakṣaṇaṃ pāśāntau samāhṛtya dakṣiṇato dakṣiṇāgner lakṣaṇam
10.1.1.10	etad eva viparyasyottarata utkarasya lakṣaṇam
10.1.1.11a	yāvat pramāṇā rajjuḥ syāt tāvad evāgamo bhavet
10.1.1.11c	āgamārdhe bhavec chaṅkuḥ śaṅkor ardhe nirāñchanam
10.1.1.12a	samantacaturasrāṇi vidhir eṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
10.1.2.1a	aṣṭāśītiḥ śatamīṣā tiryagakṣaś catuḥśatam
10.1.2.1c	ṣaḍaśītir yugaṃ cāsya rathaś cārakya ucyate
10.1.2.2a	īṣāyā lakṣaṇaṃ mītvā ṣaṭsu navasu ca lakṣaṇe
10.1.2.2c	tricatvāriṃśake pāśo 'ṅgulānāṃ niyogataḥ
10.1.2.3a	eṣā vediḥ samākhyātā cārakyarathasaṃmitā
10.1.2.3c	aindrāgnasya paśor eṣā paśuṣv anyeṣu ṣaṭśayā
10.1.2.4a	prācyardhaḥ ṣaḍaratniḥ syād ardhāratner nirāñchanam
10.1.2.4c	ardhe śroṇī tato 'rdhe 'ṃsāv adhyardha iti pāśukī
10.1.2.5a	pāśād ardhaśaye śroṇī dvayoḥ pṛṣṭhyāparā dvayoḥ
10.1.2.5c	prācyardhas tu tato 'dhyardhe tato 'dhyardhe nirāñchanam

10.1.2.5c	aratnau tu tataḥ pāśo vedī mārutī vāruṇī

10.1.2.7a	sarvā saptaśayā rajjur madhye cāsyā nirāñchanam
10.1.2.7c	prācyardhaṃ pañcame kuryād dikkuṣṭhā paitṛkī smṛtā
10.1.3.1a	prāgvaṃśaṃ daśakaṃ kuryāt patnīśālāṃ catuḥśayām
10.1.3.1c	prāgvaṃśāt triṣu vedyanto vedyantāt prakrame sadaḥ
10.1.3.2a	navakaṃ tu sado vidyāc catvāraḥ sadaso 'ntaram
10.1.3.2c	catvāras trikā havirdhānam ardhaṣaṣṭhas tad anantaram
10.1.3.3a	padaṃ yūpāvaṭe mītvā śeṣam auttaravedikam
10.1.3.3c	āgnīdhraṃ ṣaḍaratny eva ṣaṭtriṃśatprakramā rajjuḥ
10.1.3.4	lakṣikā dvādaśa trikā / vedisadohavirdhānāni minoty evānupūrvaśaḥ pañcadaśakam ekaviṃśakaṃ trikam aparaṃ parato 'paras triko dvādaśasu ca pāśada ucyate / some rajjunimānam uttamam

10.1.3.6c	ardhacaturdaśaḥ pāśaḥ sadasaś chedanam uttamam
10.1.3.7	nimāya rajjuṃ daśabhī rathākṣair ekādaśabhiś coparabudhnamātrais tasyāś caturviṃśatibhāgadheyam ekādaśinīṃ prati vedim āhuḥ
10.1.3.8a	śikhaṇḍinī cet kartavyā vedyantād dvyardham uddharet
10.1.3.8c	aṣṭāṅgulaṃ tadardhaṃ syād devyavediprasiddhaye
10.1.3.8e	taṃ prāñcaṃ tu samīkṣeta tāṃs tu vidyāc chikhaṇḍinīm
10.1.3.9a	pañcakaṃ saptakaṃ caiva ekamekaṃ tataḥ punaḥ
10.1.3.9c	eṣā vediḥ samākhyātā kaukilyās tv atha cārake
10.1.4.1a	janmanā rogahīno vā yajamāno bhaved yadi
10.1.4.1c	kathaṃ tatra pramāṇāni prayoktavyāni kartṛbhiḥ
10.1.4.2a	tuṇḍaṃ puṣkaranālasya ṣaḍguṇaṃ pariveṣṭitam
10.1.4.2c	trihāyaṇyā vatsataryā valena samamiṣyate
10.1.4.3a	trayas trihāyaṇīvālāḥ sarṣapārdhaṃ vidhīyate
10.1.4.3c	dviguṇaṃ sarṣapaṃ prāhur yavaḥ sarṣapār ...
10.1.4.4a	aṅgulasya pramāṇaṃ tu ṣaḍyavāḥ pārśvasaṃhitāḥ
10.1.4.4c	daśāṅgulas tu prādeśo vitastir dvādaśāṅgulaḥ
10.1.4.4e	dvivitastir aratniḥ syād vyāyām astu catuḥśayaḥ
10.1.4.5a	viṃśatiśatāṅgulataḥ puruṣaḥ svaiḥsvair aṅguliparvabhiḥ
10.1.4.5c	atha cet prapadotthānaḥ pañcaviṃśaśato bhavet
10.1.4.6a	triyavaṃ kṛṣṇalaṃ vidyāt taṃ mānaṃ vidyāt trikṛṣṇalam
10.1.4.6c	anena kṛṣṇalapramāṇena niṣkam āhuś caturguṇam
10.1.4.7a	puruṣasya tṛtīyapañcamau bhāgau tatkaraṇaṃ punaściteḥ
10.1.4.7c	tasyārdham athāparaṃ bhavet tricitikam agnicitiś cet

10.1.4.8	aṣṭau dvādaśa cottamā citir iti
10.2.1.1	athāta uttareṣṭakaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
10.2.1.2	ūrdhvabāhunā yajamānena veṇuṃ vimimīte
10.2.1.3	tatsamo 'nyataraḥ sāratnir dvitīyas tasya puruṣe lakṣaṇam aratnivitastyoś cobhayor ardhapuruṣe
10.2.1.4	śirasi pariśrite yūpāyāvaśiṣya śeṣam anurajju puruṣau saṃdhāya pañcāṅgyā śaṅkuṃ vinihanti tayoḥ saṃdhāv ardhayoś ca
10.2.1.5	yāv abhito madhyamaṃ śaṅkuṃ tayor veṇū nidhāya dakṣiṇataḥ puruṣasaṃnipāte todaṃ karoti
10.2.1.6	madhyame śaṅkau veṇuṃ nidhāyādhyadhi todaṃ hṛtvā dakṣiṇataḥ puruṣe śaṅkuṃ nihanti
10.2.1.7	pūrve śaṅkau veṇuṃ nidhāya dvitīyaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ purastāt puruṣasaṃnipāte śaṅkuṃ nihanty ardhe caivaṃ paścāt
10.2.1.8	etenottarārdho vyākhyātaḥ
10.2.1.9	dakṣiṇasya vargasya yāv abhito madhyamaṃ śaṅkuṃ tayor veṇū nidhāya dakṣiṇataḥ puruṣasaṃnipāte todaṃ karoti
10.2.1.10	madhyame śaṅkau veṇuṃ nidhāyādhyadhi todaṃ hṛtvā dakṣiṇataḥ sāratnau śaṅkuṃ nihanti
10.2.1.11	yaḥ sāratnis taṃ madhyamasya pūrve nidhāya dvitīyaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ purastāt sāratnim ardhapuruṣeṇa saṃnipātya śaṅkuṃ nihanty evaṃ paścāt
10.2.1.12	etenaivottarapakṣo vyākhyātaḥ
10.2.1.13	puchaṃ savitastir aratnisthāne
10.2.1.14	pūrvasya purastād ardhapuruṣeṇa pañcāṅgyā śiro vimimīte
10.2.2.1	vyāyāmasyāṣṭamam ekatas turīyam ekata ubhayatas turīyaṃ ca te gārhapatyaciteḥ karaṇe
10.2.2.2	puruṣasya daśamena bhāgena prathamaṃ caturasraṃ karaṇaṃ kārayed daśamam ekato 'rdham ekatas tad dvitīyaṃ daśamam ekato 'dhyardham ekatas tat tṛtīyam ubhayatas turīyaṃ tac caturtham
10.2.2.3	tāsām utsedhas triṃśat pañcamabhāgenānyatra nākasadbhyaś ca cūḍābhya ṛtavyābhyo 'tha madhyamāyāṃ pañcamaṣaṣṭhībhyaś ca vaiśvadevībhyas tā ardhotsedhāḥ
10.2.2.4	purīṣam antardhāyottarām upadadhyād gaṇasaṃsargāyāvichedāya
10.2.2.5	garteṣūpadadhyād yad anyad iṣṭakābhyaḥ
10.2.2.6	tatra śloko bhavati
10.2.2.6a	ukhāyāḥ paśuśīrṣāṇāṃ kūrmasyolūkhalasya ca
10.2.2.6c	srucoḥ kumbheṣṭakānāṃ ca caroś caivāvaṭān khanet
10.2.2.7	pratidiśam upadadhyād ātmani madhye prācīḥ śirasi puche pakṣayoś cātmany apyayeśu samaṃ vibhajyottarāmuttarām apyayasaṃhitāṃ pūrvāparadakṣiṇottarā viṣayavacanād anyac catasraḥ purastāt pañcartavyābhyaḥ paścāc cottarapūrve cārdhe gārhapatyasya / śeṣaṃ caturasrābhiḥ
10.2.2.8	etā eva dakṣiṇottarā dvitīyasyāṃ śeṣaṃ caturasrābhiḥ
10.2.2.9	yathā prathamaivaṃ tṛtīyā pañcamī ca yathā dvitīyaivaṃ caturthy etena dharmeṇa vyatyāsaṃ cinuyāt
10.2.2.10	athetarān āgnīdhrīyādīn navanava padāni karoty ekaikaṃ madhye 'śmānam āgnīdhrīye catvāricatvāri turīyāṇi pratidiśaṃ hotrīye catasro 'rdhāḥ kuṣṭhāsu brāhmaṇāchaṃsya itareṣāṃ dvedve adhyardhe madhye prācīḥ ṣaḍ eva mārjālīye paśuśrapaṇe ca
10.2.2.11	viṃśatim adhyardhāḥ prācīr aṃsayor dadyāc chroṇyoḥ puche ca viṃśatiṃ dvādaśadvādaśa purastāt pakṣyoḥ prācīḥ paścāc ca pañcapañca codīcīr abhitaḥ śirasi / śeṣaṃ caturasrābhiḥ
10.2.2.12	viṃśatiṃ śroṇyaṃsapakṣeṣūdīcīr dakṣiṇatas tathottarato dvitīyasyām ekādaśaikādaśābhitaḥ puche pañcapañca prācīr abhitaḥ śirasi / śeṣaṃ caturasrābhiḥ
10.2.2.13	yathā prathamaivaṃ tṛtīyā pañcamī ca yathā dvitīyaivaṃ caturthy etena dharmeṇa vyatyāsaṃ cinuyāt
10.2.2.14	trir upasatsu dve pūrvasyāṃ tisro madhyamāyāṃ ṣaṭsu yathānupūrveṇa dvādaśasu vyatyāsaṃ citipurīṣe karoti
10.2.2.15	etena dharmeṇa saṃvatsarāt samaṃ vibhajya jānudaghne 'sya dviguṇaṃ triguṇam uttareṣāṃ caikām uttarām uddhatyābhyāyanaṃ vardhāyātiriktā upadadhyāt
10.2.2.16	mantrādy abhimarśanāntaṃ tat puruṣasya lakṣaṇam
10.2.3.1	darbhastambaṃ puṣkaraparṇaṃ rukmapuruṣau hiraṇyeṣṭakāṃ śarkarāṃ svayamātṛṇṇāṃ dūrveṣṭakā naivāram iti madhyaṃ [ ā pañcam āśraṃ svayamātṛṇṇāyā abhitas tāṃ madhyaṃ ] / tasmin kumbheṣṭakā yā madhye dakṣiṇottare ca srucāv anūpamadhyeṣu śeṣāḥ paścāt svayamātṛṇṇāyāḥ kulāyinīṃ dviyajuś ca vaṃśayoḥ pārśvasaṃhite dviyajur uttare purastād retaḥsicau dve dakṣiṇe tasmin vaṃśe dvitīyām ṛtavyāṃ ca purastāc caturthe loke retaḥsicaṃ viśvajyotiṣaṃ maṇḍalām ṛtavyāṃ gharmeṣṭakām aṣāḍhāṃ kūrmaṃ vṛṣabham iti prāñcam uttare vaṃśe dakṣiṇataḥ purastāt svayamātṛṇṇāyāḥ prāñcam ulūkhalamusalam uttarapūrvye cokhāṃ madhye śirasāṃ śirobhiḥ saṃhitām upadadhāti
10.2.3.2	tasyāḥ paścāt puruṣaśirasaḥ puruṣacitim upadadhāti ṣaṭtriṃśataṃ pratīcīs trivargeṇa śroṇyām
10.2.3.3	tatra śloko bhavati
10.2.3.3a	tisro grīvāḥ ṣaḍaṃsayor dvedve bāhvor navātmani
10.2.3.3c	uṅghayoru pañca paścād ekaikaṃ pāṇipādayoḥ
10.2.3.3	iti
10.2.3.4	aṣṭāv athāpasyāḥ samaṃ vibhajya vaṃśeṣu navamenavame prāṇabhṛtaḥ purastāduttare vaṃśe prathamaṃ paścāddakṣiṇe dakṣiṇataḥ pūrva uttarataḥ paścāddakṣiṇataḥ svayamātṛṇṇāyā dvitīye pañcamam anūpeṣu saṃyato navame 'timātrā yathā prāṇabhṛtaḥ purastāddakṣiṇe vaṃśe prathamaṃ paścāduttare dakṣiṇataḥ paścāduttarataḥ pūrva uttarataḥ svayamātṛṇṇāyā dvitīye pañcamaṃ / vaiśvadevyaś cānūpeṣu pratidiśam uttarapūrveṣu vaṃśeṣvādyā / dakṣiṇottare ca saṃyānyāv apyaye tayor vaṃśayor ādyāt purastād vātharvaśiraḥ
10.2.3.5	samaṃ vibhajya vaṃśeṣu śiraḥ pakṣapuchāni prathameṣu vaṃśeṣu lokān vijānīyāt
10.2.3.6	śirasi prathame vaṃśa uttarāmuttarām itareṣāṃ pakṣapuchānāṃ caturthe pakṣayoḥ prācīḥ puche codīcīr lokeṣṭakā upadadhyāc cheṣāḥ paścāt svayamātṛṇṇāyā ekaikāṃ pūrvāṃ saṃhitāṃ dakṣiṇe vaṃśe vaiśvadevyādya uttare ca purīṣādyaḥ
10.2.3.7	gāyatraṃ madhye śirasi rathaṃtaraṃ bṛhad yajñāyajñiyam iti yathāmnātam
10.2.4.1	dvitīyāyāṃ purastāt svayamātṛṇṇāyāḥ prathamadvitīyatṛtīyeṣv ṛtavyā vāyavyā apasyā iti yathāsaṃkhyaṃ tisrastisro dakṣiṇeṣu vaṃśeṣu dakṣiṇottarā dvedve uttarasyottarayor navame 'bhitaḥ śeṣā yathāpasyāḥ
10.2.4.2	tṛtīyāyāṃ daśa dvādaśa namave 'bhito 'ṣṭame sapta purastāt paścāc ca samīcīr abhitaḥ svayamātṛṇṇāyā ardhotsedhā aṣṭau nānāmantrā uttamāyāṃ vā
10.2.4.3	caturthyām ekaikāṃ navamenavame 'bhitaḥ purastāduttarasya vaṃśasya madhye prathamāṃ vyatyāsam itarā evam eva spṛtaḥ purastāddakṣiṇasya vaṃśasya madhye prathamāṃ vyatyāsam itarāḥ / ṣaṭsaptāṣṭameṣu dakṣiṇato yugmāyugmā uttaratas trivargān kuryāt saptadaśa dakṣiṇataḥ pañcadaśottarataḥ
10.2.4.4	pañcamyām ekaikāṃ prāṇabhṛdādhiṣu śeṣaṃ chandasāṃ virājaś ca yathātimātrāḥ ṣaṭsaptāṣṭameṣv abhito yathāsaṃkhyam
10.2.4.5	ardheṣṭakābhiḥ pūrayitvā dakṣiṇataḥ prācīḥ stomabhāgāḥ paścimāś ca yugmā uttaratas trivargān kuryād ekatriṃśataṃ paścāt pratyañcaṃ trivargeṇa nākasadaṃ ca paścāt purīṣavatyā yavādinā sanāmnīr upaśīvarīr ghṛtaplutā iti yathāsaṃkhyaṃ turīyāṇi madhye yathā prāṇabhṛto 'timātrā madhyamāṃ svayamātṛṇṇāsaṃhitām uttaratas tu vikarṇīm
10.2.4.6	iti suparṇasya
10.2.5.1a	yāvatī śoṣapākābhyām iṣṭakā hrasate kṛtā
10.2.5.1c	tāvat samadhikaṃ kāryaṃ karaṇaṃ samam ichatā
10.2.5.2a	sadā ca triṃśakaṃ bhāgam iṣṭakā hrasate kṛtā
10.2.5.2c	tāvat samadhikaṃ kāryaṃ karaṇaṃ samam ichatā
10.2.5.3a	ekaikaṃ śatam adhyardhaṃ tad ūtaṃ ṣaḍbhir aṅgulaiḥ
10.2.5.3c	iṣṭakānāṃ parimāṇaṃ vaikṛtaṃ yadato 'nyathā
10.2.5.4a	navāṅgulasahasrāṇi dve śate ṣoḍaśottare
10.2.5.4c	aṅgulānāṃ parimāṇaṃ vyāyāmasya tu nirdiśet
10.2.5.5a	itareṣāṃ tu dhiṣṇyānāṃ sarveṣām eva niścayaḥ
10.2.5.5c	ekaikasya sahasraṃ syācchate ṣaṇṇavatiḥ parā
10.2.5.6a	ekādaśa sahasrāṇi aṅgulānāṃ śatāni ṣaṭ
10.2.5.6c	śataṃ caiva sahasrāṇāṃ kṣetram agner vidhīyate
10.2.5.7a	prākṛtaṃ vaikṛtaṃ vāpi kṣetram ardhāṣṭamāntare
10.2.5.7c	pañcaviṃśaṃ śiraḥ kṛtvā tataḥ kṣetre samāvapet
10.2.5.8a	śatāny aṣṭau padonāni padānām iha kīrtyante
10.2.5.8c	sāṅgasya saśiraskasya kṣetraṃ kṣetravido viduḥ
10.2.5.9a	ātmā catuḥśataḥ kāryaḥ pakṣau triṃśacchatau smṛtau
10.2.5.9c	daśa puche śataṃ caiva śiraḥ syāt pañcaviṃśakam
10.2.5.10a	ekatriṃśas trayastriṃśair vargaiḥ pañcāśakairapi
10.2.5.10c	asaṃbhavatsu vargeṣu dvidhā bhidyeta iṣṭakā
10.2.5.11a	iṣṭakāhrasavṛddhibhyāṃ dṛdhāsu śatakeṣu ca
10.2.5.11c	matimān iṣṭakā bhāgair mantrāt saṃnāśayed iti
10.2.5.12a	caturasre pṛṣṭau vāpi pakṣapuchaśireṣṭakāḥ
10.2.5.12c	dikto 'padhānaṃ lokāc ca tathā lokas tu lupyate
10.2.5.13a	adhyātmani ha vijñeyam upadhānaṃ vijānatā
10.2.5.13c	rathaṃtarabṛhallokair anyaṃ gāyatrayājñiyaiḥ
10.2.5.14a	yajuṣmatīnāṃ saṃkhyā tu sarvāsāṃ caiva niścitā
10.2.5.14c	ekaikasyāṃ citau vāpi tāṃ me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
10.2.5.15a	ṣaḍaśītiḥ śataṃ tv ādyā dvitīyā daśa saptatiḥ
10.2.5.15c	trayodaśa tṛtīyā syācchataṃ cāhur manīṣiṇaḥ
10.2.5.15a	caturthī śatam ekā syāt tisraś caiveṣṭakāḥ smṛtāḥ
10.2.5.15c	śatāni trīṇi pañcāśat ṣaṭ caiva citir uttamā
10.2.5.16a	etāḥ sarvā yajuṣmatyo yābhir agniḥ prasūyate
10.2.5.16c	śeṣaṃ lokaṃpṛṇābhis tu citīnām abhipūrayet
10.2.5.17a	etāḥ sarvā samāmnātāḥ yajur yāvat pravartate
10.2.5.17c	tad etad dhi sahasraṃ syāccharkarābhiḥ sahocyate
10.2.5.18a	etā upahitāḥ samyag dhenavas tu prajāyante

10.3.2.1a	janmanā rogahīno vā yajamāno bhaved yadi
10.3.2.1c	kathaṃ tatra pramāṇāni prayoktavyāni kartṛbhiḥ
10.3.2.2	yady urutantuḥ keśo vāstṛtaḥ sarṣapo yavaś caiva ṣaḍguṇitaḥṣaḍguṇito bhavati narasyāṅgulaṃ māne taddvādaśakaṃ prādeśam ity āhuḥ
10.3.2.3	taddvayaṃ smṛto 'ratniḥ prakramo 'ratnisamaḥ sa dviḥprādeśo bhavec citiṣu

10.3.2.6	ekasyāṃ vedyām agnidvayam iṣṭakāriktaṃ bhavati / pṛthag ato vediḥ cet pṛthag agniḥ kl̥ptaḥ
10.3.2.7	viṃśatyaṅgulaḥ śataṃ niyataḥ pañcāratnir naro daśapado vā / hīnātiriktayuktyā dehedehe pramāṇaṃ tu
10.3.2.8	ṣaḍaśītir yugam uktaṃ sāṣṭādaśa ucyate tvakṣas tantrasamasamastaṃ dvyujaṃ ratham īṣāṃ vyavāsyanti
10.3.2.9	maṇḍalam atha caturasraṃ maṇḍalaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt tasyemaṃ karaṇavidhiṃ tadvidām udāhṛtaṃ śṛṇuta
10.3.2.10	maṇḍalaviṣkambhasamas tribhujād avalambakaś catuḥsraktiḥ prāgāyatāt tribhāgāt karṇāt sa maṇḍalaṃ bhavati
10.3.2.11	puruṣaḥ puruṣaṃ kuryāt tasyākṣṇayā dvipuruṣaṃ bhavec caturastasyāpyakṣṇayā dvābhyāṃ vā syāś catuḥpuruṣam
10.3.2.12	dvipuruṣaḥ karaṇī śroṇī bāhus tu dviguṇo bhavet triṃkuṣṭhavat tryavalambakas tato yaś caturasre dvāṣṭamāḥ puruṣāḥ
10.3.2.13a	viṣkambhaḥ pañcabhāgaś ca viṣkambhas triguṇaś ca yaḥ
10.3.2.13c	sa maṇḍalaparikṣepo na vālam atiricyate
10.3.2.14a	daśadhā chidya viṣkambhaṃ tribhāgān uddharet tataḥ
10.3.2.14c	tena yac caturasraṃ syān maṇḍale tadapaprathiḥ
10.3.2.15a	caturasraṃ navadhā kuryād dhanuḥkoṭyas tridhātridhā
10.3.2.15c	utsedhāt pañcamaṃ lumpet purīṣeṇeha tāvat samam
10.3.2.16	caturaratnir vā naraḥ sikatākaraṇe tv ardhaṃ bhujaḥ pradiśyate
10.3.2.17	karaṇāni tato 'syāḥ kārayet tricatuḥpañca trir abhiparyasya yac chubhaṃ cayaneṣu vidhiḥ purātanair ṛṣibhir yo 'bhihitaś ca nityaśaḥ
10.3.2.18	parilekhanamānasaṃcayair vyatyāsaiḥ parimāṇasaṃpadā vedyaḥ sarvāḥ pramāṇair āyāmena ca vistareṇa ca mimīyāt
10.3.2.19	caturasrasaṃpadā dvayāyām asamāpanāḥ smṛtā pañcāṅgyātha vā purātanair yāḥ pūrvair ṛṣibhiḥ pradarśitāḥ
10.3.2.20a	yaś caiṣa vidhir maryākṛtas tatraiṣā mithunāt samam

10.3.2.22	prācīm athāyāmasamāṃ nidadhyāt pāśau nikhanyād atha madhyamaṃ ca
10.3.2.23	unmucya paścād atha madhyame tat prāgdakṣiṇāyamya nirāñchanena vistārato 'rdhe nikhaneta śaṅkuṃ pratyak tathottaramadhyame ca / sa vāsuvedīṣu
10.3.2.24	atha mānam etac chroṇyāṃ tu pāśoddharaṇaṃ kriyeta
10.3.2.25	aṃsaśroṇyor likheta dikṣu lekhāḥ śaṅkū nihanyāt samareṣu teṣu / tebhyaḥ samantāt parilekhayeta

10.3.4.17a	iṣṭakā śoṣapākābhyāṃ triṃśanmānāt tu hīyate

10.3.5.1	saptatriṃśatsārdhāḥ pakṣaḥ savyaś ca śirasi catvāraḥ ṣaḍviṃśakas tathātmā śyene pañcadaśakaṃ puchaṃ saptadaśakaṃ puchaṃ dvayaṃ śirasy ātmapakṣayoḥ kl̥ptam alajasya / bhāgasaṃdhāntayajñaiḥ pratimā naracaturthe
10.3.5.2	aṣṭau bhāgāḥ puchaṃ kaṅkacite bhavati pādayoś caturaḥ śirasi tu sapta jñeyāḥ śyenavad ātmā ca pakṣau ca
10.3.5.3	śyenālajakaṅkānām aṣṭau sārdhā vistṛtaṃ puchaṃ catvāro tmā dvau ca śiraḥ sarveṣāṃ pñcakau pakṣau
10.3.5.4	śyenālajakaṅkānāṃ dvitricatuḥ kuṣṭham ity ucyate puchaṃ pañcākṣṇāḥ pakṣapātrās tvakṣṇābhiḥ pariśritāḥ

10.3.6.6a	maṇḍalacaturasro 'dya parivāryaḥ śmaśānacit
10.3.6.6c	droṇacit tsarumāneṣāṃ daśabhāgo bhavet tsaruḥ
10.3.6.7a	maṇḍale caturasraṃ tu kuryād gārhapatyavat
10.3.6.7c	bāhvor viṃśatibhāgena vāruṇaṃ sārdham eva tu
10.3.6.8a	prasiddhaṃ daśadhā kuryād bahir antaś ca yuktitaḥ
10.3.6.8c	trikuṣṭhaś ca viṣāṇaḥ syāt saṃdhau vyatyāsa eva saḥ
10.3.6.9a	caturasrasya karaṇaṃ bāhvor dvātriṃśadbhāgikam
10.3.6.9c	caturasram athādhyardhaṃ tābhyāṃ gāyatravadvidhiḥ
10.3.6.10a	sāhasrasya karaṇaṃ bāhvoḥ pañcadaśabhāgaṃ caturasram
10.3.6.10c	adhyardhās tu tataḥ syur dviśatāś citayaḥ smṛtāḥ
10.3.6.11a	pañca pañcāśatam adhyardhās tisraḥ pañcāśataṃ caturasrāḥ
10.3.6.11c	sahasrāc chataṃ pakṣāḥ syur uṣā sahasratamī
10.3.6.12a	bāhvor ekatriṃśo bhāgaḥ karaṇaṃ citis tathottarayoḥ
10.3.6.12c	caturasrānāṃ sāhasraṃ savanike vyavāsyanti
10.3.6.13	ardhaikādaśapuruṣaṃ ghanaṃ bhaved bhaven maṇḍalaṃ rathacakraṃ / nābhir arā vivaradhā nemir arebhyo yady atiriktam
10.3.6.14	tadardhāḥ puruṣāyāmāḥ puruṣāṣṭabhāgavistṛtāḥ caturviṃśatis trinaranāyāḥ
10.3.6.15	vivarakaraṇamataḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi / dvisaptamena nemyasrakaraṇaṃ bhaved arasyāṣṭabhāgena vaikṛtaś caturviṃśatibhāgena nābhyām antaram antaro 'ṣṭamabhāgena praugavad bhavet
10.3.6.16a	dvīṣṭakāṃ cinuyān nābhiṃ caturbhiś cinuyād arān
10.3.6.16c	tribhir nemiṃ yathābhāgaṃ / vyatyāsaḥ kūpavat smṛtaḥ
10.3.6.17a	viṣkambhasya caturthena nābhyās tu vivaraṃ likhet
10.3.6.17c	tricatvāriṃśāṅgulāṃ nemiṃ sārdhacaturaṅgulām
10.3.6.18a	siddham anyad yathā yuktiś cayane yāś ca saṃpadaḥ
10.3.6.19	ya idam api yathātathaṃ smṛtiṃ vidhiṃ yad ādhītya mimīte rauravaṃ samavati khalu kṛtsnasaṃmato vrajati ca śulbakṛtāṃ salokatām
10.3.7.1a	rathacakrasya cityasya saṃkṣepoktasya viṣṇunā
10.3.7.1c	atha dhātur niviṣṭhasya triguṇānyaṃ bahirbahiḥ
10.3.7.1e	līyante maṇḍale yasya sapta sārdhā narā budhaiḥ
10.3.7.2a	mucyante vivareṣv anye kṣetrād abhyadhikās trayaḥ
10.3.7.3a	tasya cakravidhānaṃ tu / nemir arebhyo vistaraḥ
10.3.7.3c	maṇḍalānāṃ ca viṣkambhaḥ tribhāgaḥ karaṇāni ca
10.3.7.4a	narārdhenābhilikhen nābhis tataḥ prastāragocarā
10.3.7.4c	arebhyo 'bhyadhikā nemis triṣaṣṭhenākṣarāgāram
10.3.7.4a	triṃśatena saviṃśena adhikaiś cārdhapañcamaiḥ
10.3.7.4c	mimāyāṅgulair vā madhyaṃ kuryād viṃśena parilekhanam
10.3.7.5a	prathame prastare rathacakrasya śṛṇuteṣṭakāḥ
10.3.7.5c	caturbhir adhikaṃ vettha catvāriṃśac chatatrayam
10.3.7.6a	dvitīye 'bhyadhikā yāntu caturviṃśatir iṣṭakāḥ
10.3.7.6c	pañcakoṇās trikoṇāś ca nemyarebhyaḥ ca saṃdhiṣu
10.3.7.7a	iṣṭakānāṃ sahasreṇa śataiḥ saptabhir eva ca
10.3.7.7c	aṣṭaṣaṣṭyā ca cakrasya citayaḥ pañca pūritāḥ
11.1.1.1	athātaḥ pratigrahakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.1.1.2	dakṣiṇāṃ pratigṛhṇīyād nāvedavin nāśucir nāyajñopavītī na muktaśikho nārtaś ca nānudake na cākāle
11.1.1.3	sāvitraḥ purastāt ka idam iti paścāt
11.1.1.4	prajāpataye tveti puruṣīṃ pratigṛhṇīyād dhastinaṃ puruṣaṃ bhūmiṃ prāṇi cānyat sarvaṃ jīvam anūrvarāṃ candrāya tveti śiro yamāya tvety ekaśaphaṃ rudrāya tveti gām agnaye tveti hiraṇyaṃ trapu sīsamayo lohaṃ ca gnās tvākṛntann apaso 'tanvata dhiyo 'vayan bṛhaspataye tveti vāsa uttānāya tvety aprāṇad viśvebhyo devebhyas tveti chattraṃ gṛhaṃ grāmaṃ ca śrīkāmāya tveti śayyām indrāgnibhyāṃ tveti chāgaṃ meṣaṃ mahiṣaṃ ca varuṇāya tvety udakumbhaṃ kūpaṃ taḍāgaṃ ca samudrāya tveti karakaśaṅkhaśuktipravālāni yac cānyat kiṃcit sāmudraṃ tvaṣṭra ity uṣṭrān somāya rasān dravān gandhasrajo vanaspatīṃś ca vaiśvānarāya tveti tveti rathān
11.1.1.5	yady āsaṃbhṛtā nānādakṣiṇās tāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt
11.1.1.5a	pṛthivyāṃ puṇyaṃ ca pāpaṃ ca kas te pratipaśyati
11.1.1.5c	iṣṭapuṇyaṃ ca pāpaṃ ca ādityaḥ pratipaśyati
11.1.1.5a	yadā dātā pramīyeta yasmai dattaṃ sa jīvati
11.1.1.5c	antarāvartamānābhyāṃ dakṣiṇā kasya tiṣṭhati
11.1.1.5a	varuṇo dakṣiṇāḥ pratigṛhya viṣṭāve prayachati
11.1.1.5c	sa dātā sarvasatyānāṃ janmakāle punaḥpunaḥ
11.1.1.5	iti
11.1.2.1	puruṣīṃ haste gṛhītvā prasāre vīraṃ bāhubhyāṃ bāhukārīm abhiruhya hastinaṃ puruṣaṃ bhūmiṃ pṛṣṭhe 'śvaṃ gāṃ puche hiraṇyaṃ gṛhītvā vāsaḥ paridhāyākramyāprāṇaṃ chattraṃ daṇḍe ratham īṣāyāṃ grāmaṃ madhye gṛhaṃ praviśya śayyām āruhyājaṃ karṇe meṣam ūrṇāyāṃ mahiṣaṃ śṛṅga udakumbhaṃ gṛhītvā kūpam avalokya taḍāgam avatīrya karakaśaṅkhaśuktipravālāni gṛhītvā yac cānyat kiṃcit sāmudraṃ śaṅkunā coṣṭrān pratodena kharān aśvatarān utkṣipya rasān anulihya gandhān sragdāmāni cāruhya vanaspatīn annaṃ gṛhītvā
11.1.2.2	śrāvyamantro brāhmaṇasya japamantro rājanyasyopāṃśumantro vaiśyasya śūdrasya gṛhān niṣkramya bahir upaspṛśya manasā mantram āvartayet
11.1.2.3	ya evaṃ vidvān pratigṛhṇāti punāti dātāraṃ punāti cātmānaṃ punāti dakṣiṇā deveṣu vettāham iti
11.2.1	athāto mūlajātasya vidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.2.2	mūlasya prathame 'ṃśe pitur neṣṭo dvitīye mātus tṛtīye dhanasya caturthe kulaśokāvaha ātmano vā puṇyabhāgī bhavati
11.2.3	tatrodakumbhaṃ kuryāt tasmin rudrāñ japitvāpratirathaṃ rakṣoghnaṃ sūktaṃ ca
11.2.4	dvitīyodakumbhaś catuḥprasravaṇasaṃyuktas tasmin mūlāni dhārayed vaṃśayātrākṛtāni
11.2.5	teṣāṃ pradhānāni mūlāni vakṣyāmi / prathamāḥ kāśmaryaḥ sahadevī aparājitā adhaḥpuṣpī śaṅkhapuṣpī balā pāṭalā mayūraśikhā madhupuṣpikā cakrāṅkitā kākajaṅghā kumārī dvitīyā vaijayantī apāmārgo bhṛṅgarajo lakṣmaṇā jātī vyāghraḥ pattrakaḥ cakramardaḥ kapileśvarā aśvatthaḥ sahaḥ palāśa udumbaraḥ plakṣaḥ śamī arko rohitako bilva ity evamādīni mūlaśaḥ pūrayitvā madhye mūlaṃ hemamayaṃ ca kuryāt saptadhānyasaṃyuktam
11.2.6	teṣāṃ niṣiddhāni mūlāni vakṣyāmi / tilvako dhavo nimbaḥ śālmalī rājavṛkṣaḥ śleṣmantakaḥ sarvakaṇṭakivarjam
11.2.7	tatrābhiṣekaṃ kurvīta pituḥ śiśor jananyā devarasyākṛtyāsandyām āsīnānāṃ saṃpātenābhiṣiñcati śiraso 'dhy ā mukhāt
11.2.8	śiro me śrīr yaśa iti yathāliṅgam aṅgāni saṃmṛśati
11.2.9	snātānām upariṣṭān nairṛtaṃ payasi sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā kāśmaryamayaṃ paridhim idhmaṃ sruksruvaṃ saṃmṛjyāghārāv ājyabhāgau hutvāsunvantam ayajamānam iti catasraḥ sthālīpākasya hutvā kayā śubhā savayasa iti pañcadaśājyāhutīr juhuyān mā nas toka iti yā te rudra śivā tanūr iti pañca
11.2.10	agne rakṣā sīsena tantram iti dvābhyāṃ sviṣṭakṛte hutvā samāpte kṛṣṇā gauḥ kṛṣṇāś ca nīlā hemamayaṃ mūlaṃ saptadhānyaṃ cācāryāya dadyād brahmaṇe kṛṣṇo 'naḍvān yathāśaktyā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ suvarṇaṃ dadyāt
11.2.11	brāhmaṇān bhojayet kṛsarapāyasānnam ājyasaṃyuktam
11.2.12	sarvaṃ śobhanaṃ kṣemam ārogyaṃ sarvāśiṣaḥ saṃpadā sarvam aṅgalasaṃpadā ca
11.2.13	evaṃ nairṛtadevate garayoge ca vidhir manunādiṣṭaḥ / śāntikarākṣe makarī śubhakarā dhanadhānya ṛddhikarī sarvakularakṣaṇī bhayaśokāpahāriṇī balabhāgye śubhakāreti
11.3.1	atha yamalaśāntiḥ
11.3.2	asya yamalau putrau gāvau vaḍave vāyāyātām
11.3.3	saṃvatsare pūrṇe dvādaśavatsare vā dvādaśarātre vā sapta karṣāyān āhared aśvattham udumbaraṃ vikaṅkataṃ nyagrodhaplakṣaśamīśamakapriyaṅgugaurasarpāṃś ca
11.3.4	yadi tān na vinded dhiraṇyasnānaṃ // hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucaya iti catasṛbhiś catuṣpāde bhadrapīṭhe prāṅmukhān upaveśya mṛnmayena śatadhāreṇa baijalaṃ sahasradhāram antardhāya yā oṣadhayaḥ sam anyā yantīty anuvākābhyāṃ catasro vidhavāḥ snāpayeyuś catvāro vā brahmacāriṇaḥ
11.3.5	snātāv alaṃkṛtau dampatī pradakṣiṇam agniṃ pariṇayet
11.3.6	paścād agner darbheṣūpaviśya mārutasya sthālīpākasya priyavatībhyāṃ sapta kṛtvo 'vadyañ juhoti
11.3.7	ṛṣabhaikā gāvo dakṣiṇā
11.3.8	purastād agneḥ sapta karṣūn khātvā tān gandhodakena pūrayitvā jayaprabhṛtibhiś cājyasya purastāt sviṣṭakṛto hiraṇyagarbha ity aṣṭābhiḥ pratyṛcam atikrāmed aṣṭamīṃ japet
11.3.9	āhitāgneś codanena vidhinā vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.3.10	mārutaṃ trayodaśakapālaṃ nirvapet
11.3.11	tasya gaur dhenur dakṣiṇā
11.3.12	yadi tāṃ na vindet sukṣetraṃ susamṛddhaṃ dadyād yavakṣetraṃ tilakṣetraṃ vā
11.3.13	yadi tāni na vindel lomavastratvagavachanno vāḍavāgniṃ praviśet sa etasyānugrahaḥ
11.4.1	athāta āśleṣāvidhimṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.4.2	prathame pāde mātṛnāśaś caturthe pitur vināśaḥ
11.4.3	tatra mūlavidhānoktauṣadhiśataṃ gṛhītvā tamrapātre parivaṃśapātre nidhāya taṇḍulān pariṣṭhāpya tasyopari hema niṣkapramāṇaṃ sarpam adhomukhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya pañcagavyena snapanaṃ kṛtvā vastrayugmena veṣṭayed yajñopavītena sugandhaiḥ pañcavarṇapuṣpair dhūpadīpair nānābhakṣabhojyopahārais tāmbūlādibhir nānāvidhaphalaiś ca
11.4.4	namo astu sarpebhya iti suvarṇasarpaṃ pūjayet
11.4.5	tataś caturaḥ kumbhān pratiṣṭhāpya prathamaṃ nirjharodakenetarān api saṃpūrya tatra prathame sapta mṛttikā dvitīye devadāru mustāṃ ca siddhārthotpalaharidrāguḍūcīcandanaṃ tṛtīye sarvauṣadhyaś caturthe sarvam idaṃ kṛtvā samudraṃ gacheti caturbhir mantrair abhimantrya gandhapuṣpādibhir arcayitvā śubhe 'hni śubhanakṣatre śubhalagne śubhavelāyāṃ yajamānaḥ śucir bhūtvāhate vāsasī paridhāya gandhādyair alaṃkṛtam ācāryaṃ namaskṛtyartvigbhiḥ saha puṇyāhavācanaṃ kṛtvā kalaśeṣu madhye sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvāgnaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvāghārāv ājyabhāgābhyāṃ hutvā tataḥ sāvitryā savitre vayaṃ someti somāyāsunvantam ayajamānam iti nirṛtaye sahasraśīrṣeti viṣṇave pṛthagaṣṭottaraśataṃ juhuyāt
11.4.6	namo astu sarpebhya iti samiccarutilājyair juhuyāt
11.4.7	sviṣṭakṛtaṃ prāyaścittāhutīr hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ hutvācāryaḥ śiśuṃ mātaraṃ pitaraṃ sarvauṣadhitilasarṣapasaṃyuktam udakaṃ kalaśād uddhṛtyartvigbhiḥ saha caturbhiḥ kalaśair abhiṣiñcet
11.4.8	pūrvavaddakṣiṇeti śeṣo vyākhyātaḥ
11.5.1	śaṅkara uvāca
11.5.1a	dantajanmani bālānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tan nibodhaye
11.5.1c	upari prathamaṃ yasya jāyante ca śiśor dvijāḥ
11.5.1a	dantair vā saha yasya syāj janma bhārgava sattama
11.5.1c	mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cātha khāded ātmānam eva vā
11.5.2a	tatra śāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi tāṃ me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
11.5.2c	gajapṛṣṭhagataṃ bālaṃ nausthaṃ vā sthāpayed dvijaḥ
11.5.2e	tadabhāvena dharmajñaḥ kāñcane ca varāsane
11.5.3a	sarvauṣadhaiḥ sarvagandhaiḥ bījaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalais tathā
11.5.3c	pañcagavyena ratnaiś ca patākābhiś ca bhārgava
11.5.3e	sthālīpākena dhātāraṃ pūjayet tadanantaram
11.5.4a	saptāhaṃ cātra kartavyaṃ tathā brāhmaṇabhojanam
11.5.4c	aṣṭame 'hani viprāṇāṃ tathā deyā ca dakṣiṇā
11.5.4e	kāñcanaṃ rajataṃ cātra bhuvam ātmānam eva ca
11.5.5a	dantajanmani sāmānye śṛṇu snānam ataḥ param
11.5.6a	bhadrāsane niveśyainaṃ mṛdbhir mūlaiḥ phalais tathā
11.5.6c	sarvauṣadhaiḥ sabījaiś ca sarvagandhais tathaiva ca
11.5.6a	snāpayet pūjayaṃś cātra vahnisomaṃ samīraṇam
11.5.6c	prathamaṃ sthāpayet tatra devadevaṃ ca keśavam
11.5.7a	teṣām eva tu juhuyād ghṛtam agnau yathāvidhi
11.5.7c	brāhmaṇānāṃ ca dātavyā tataḥ pūjā ca dakṣiṇā
11.5.8a	bhāsantaṃ chattram ūrdhānaṃ bījaiḥ susnāpayet tataḥ
11.5.8c	susnigdhair bālakānāṃ ca taiś ca kāyaṃ prapūjanam
11.5.9a	pūjyāś cāvidhavā nāryo brāhmaṇāḥ suhṛdas tathā
11.6.1a	akālaprasavā nāryaḥ kālātītaprajās tathā
11.6.1c	amānuṣā abhaṇḍāś ca ajātavyaṃjanās tathā
11.6.1a	hīnāṅgā adhikāṅgāś ca jāyante yadi vā striyaḥ
11.6.1c	paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaś caiva tathaiva ca sarīsṛpāḥ
11.6.1a	vināśaṃ tasya deśasya kulasya ca vinirdiśet
11.6.2a	nirvāsayet tān nṛpatiḥ svarāṣṭrāt striyaś ca pūjyāś ca tato dvijendrāḥ
11.6.3a	phalādikair brāhmaṇatarpaṇaṃ ca loke tataḥ śāntim upaiti prāptaḥ
11.7.1.1	athāto rudrajapasya vidhānakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.7.1.2	uttarato grāmasya purastād vā śucau deśe nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taḍāge vā malāpakarṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kuryāt
11.7.1.3	rudrasnānaṃ kurvīta
11.7.1.4	namaḥ śaṃbhave ceti snātvāsaṃkhyātā sahasrāṇīti daśabhir mārjanam uttīrya vastre ca paridhāyācamya rudraṃ nyased yā te rudreti śikhāyāṃ ye asmin mahaty arṇava iti śirasy asaṃkhyātā iti lalāṭe namo nīlakapardāyeti cakṣuṣor namaḥ śrutāya ca śrutasenāya ceti karṇayor avatatya dhanuṣ ṭvam iti mukhe namo nīlagrīvāyeti kaṇṭhe namas tā āyudhāyānātatāyeti bāhvor namo girikebhya iti hṛdaye hiraṇyagarbha iti nābhyāṃ namo gaṇebhya iti pṛṣṭau namo mīḍhuṣṭarāya ceti kaṭyām imā rudrāya tavasa iti guhye mā no mahāntam ity ūrvor ye pathāṃ pathirakṣaya iti pādayor adhyavocad iti kavacaṃ namo bilmine cety upakavacaṃ pramuñca dhanvana ity astram
11.7.1.5	ya etāvanta iti digbandhaḥ
11.7.1.6	oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāyeti vinyaset
11.7.1.6a	oṃkāraṃ mūrdhni vinyasya nakāraṃ nāsike tathā
11.7.1.6c	mokāraṃ tu lalāṭe vai bhakāraṃ mukhamadhyataḥ
11.7.1.6a	gakāraṃ kaṇṭhadeśe tu vakāraṃ hṛdaye nyaset
11.7.1.6c	tekāraṃ dakṣiṇe haste rukāraṃ vāmato nyaset
11.7.1.6e	drākāraṃ nābhimadhye tu yakāraṃ pādayos tathā
11.7.1.7	trātāram indraṃ prācīdigadhipataya indrāya namaḥ // tvaṃ no agna āgneyadigadhipataye 'gnaye namaḥ // sugaṃ nu panthāṃ dakṣiṇādigadhipataye yamāya namaḥ // asunvantam ayajamānaṃ nairṛtyadigadhipataye nirṛtaye namaḥ // tat tvā yāmi paścimadigadhipataye varuṇāya namaḥ // ā no niyudbhir vāyavyadigadhipataye vāyave namaḥ // tvaṃ soma kratubhir udagdigadhipataye kuberāya namaḥ // tam īśānam īśānadigadhipataya īśānāya namaḥ // imā rudrāya tavasa ūrdhvādigadhipataye brahmaṇe namaḥ // syonā pṛthivy adhodigadhipataye 'nantāya nama ity etad diksaṃpuṭam
11.7.1.8	evam evātmani raudrīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tvagasthigataiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyate
11.7.1.9	anena vidhinā na grāme na strīsravaṇe na śrāddha āmantrite na paśusaṃnidhau yakṣarākṣasabhūtapretapiśācayamadūtaśākinītaskarādyupaghātāḥ
11.7.1.10	sarve te jvalantaṃ paśyanti
11.7.1.11	ātmānaṃ rudrarūpaṃ dhyāyet
11.7.1.12	trinetraṃ pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ saumyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaṃ nīlagrīvaṃ śaśāṅkacihnaṃ śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ nāgayajñopavītinaṃ vyāghracarmottarīyakaṃ kamaṇḍalvakṣasūtrahastam abhayapradaṃ triśūlahastaṃ pinākapāṇinaṃ vṛṣabhaskandhasamārūḍham umādehārdhadhāriṇaṃ jvalantaṃ kapilajaṭaṃ jaṭāmukuṭasaṃyuktaṃ śikhām uddyotakāriṇam amṛtenāplutaṃ hṛṣṭaṃ surāsurair namaskṛtaṃ digdevataiḥ samāyuktaṃ nityaṃ ca śāśvataṃ śivaṃ dhruvam akṣayam avyayaṃ sarvavyāpinirañjanam īśānaṃ rudraṃ viśvarūpiṇam evaṃ dhyātvā dvijaḥ samyak tato japam ārabhet
11.7.1.13	suguptadeśe gocarmamātre 'sthansv anulipte vā liṅgapadmākṛtiṃ prakalpya prokṣya mā no mahāntam iti sthāpayed namaḥ śaṃbhave cety arcayet
11.7.1.14	sadyavāmāghoratatpuruṣeśāneti rudrasyāvāhanaṃ // sadyo jāta ity asya sadyojāta ṛṣir brahmā devatā triṣṭup chandaḥ haṃsavāhanaḥ paścimavaktraḥ pṛthivī tattvaḥ brahmarūpāya hrāṃ paścimavaktrāvāhane viniyogaḥ sadyo jātaḥ paścimavaktrāya nama ā vāhayāmi // vāmam adya savitar ity asya vāmadeva ṛṣiḥ viṣṇur devatā triṣṭup chando garuḍavāhana uttaravaktra āpas tattvo viṣṇurūpāya hrīm uttaravaktrāvāhane viniyogo vāmam adya savitar uttaravaktrāya nama ā vāhayāmi // aghorebhya ity asyāghora ṛṣī rudro devatā bṛhatī chando vṛṣabhavāhano dakṣiṇavaktras tejas tattvo rudrarūpāya hrūṃ dakṣiṇavaktrāvāhane viniyogo aghorebhyo dakṣiṇavaktrāya namas ā vāhayāmi // tatpuruṣāyety asya tatpuruṣa ṛṣiḥ sūryo devatā gāyatrī chando 'śvavāhanaḥ pūrvavaktro vāyus tattvaḥ sūryarūpāya hraiṃ pūrvavaktrāvāhane viniyogas tatpuruṣāya pūrvavaktrāya nama ā vāhayāmi // tam īśānam ity asyeśāna ṛṣiḥ śabdo devatā bṛhatī chandaḥ kūrmavāhana ūrdhvavaktra ākāśatattvaḥ śvetarūpāya hraum ūrdhvavaktrāvāhane viniyogas tam īśānam ūrdhvavaktrāya nama ā vāhayāmi // ā tvā vahantv iti rudragāyatrīm aṣṭau kṛtvaḥ prayuñjīta
11.7.1.15	rudraṃ dhyāyet
11.7.1.16	nīlakaṇṭhaṃ mahādevaṃ kailāsasthaṃ sahomayā trinetram īśvaraṃ caiva dhyātvā siddhim avāpnuyāt
11.7.1.17	tato japam ārabhed namas te rudra manyava iti prabhṛtibhir aṣṭābhir anuvākaiḥ
11.7.1.18	prathamānuvāke gāyatrī chandas tisras triṣṭubhas tisraḥ paṅktayaḥ saptānuṣṭubho 'ntyānuvāke prathamā bṛhatī dve triṣṭubhau dvādaśānuṣṭubho dve jagatyau
11.7.1.19	śeṣānāṃ nānāchandasāṃ rudrānāṃ rudro devatā ghora ṛṣiḥ
11.7.1.20	śatarudriyāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ sarvapāpakṣayārthe jape viniyogaḥ
11.7.1.21	namas te rudra manyava ityādir aṣṭānuvākāḥ
11.7.1.22	asaṃkhyātā sahasrāṇīti yathāliṅgaṃ sthāpanaṃ dhyātvā namo astu rudrebhyo ye divīty aṃsadaghne dhyāyed namo astu rudrebhyo ye antarikṣa iti nābhidaghne namo astu rudrebhyo ye pṛthivyām iti jānudaghne dhyāyet
11.7.1.23	aghorebhya iti japitvā yaḥ patha iti visarjayet
11.7.1.24	apratirathaṃ japan gṛham āvrajet
11.7.1.25	tenodakenātmānam abhiṣiñcet
11.7.1.26	dvipadaś catuṣpadaś cetann ity ajapasya vidhānam
11.7.2.1	naimittikasya punar vakṣyāmi
11.7.2.2	pūrvoktena vidhinā snātvā nyāsaṃ kṛtvā śaṅkha udakaṃ gṛhītvā yathālābhe pātre vā dūrvāpuṣpā ekodakam akṣatam īśānābhimukhaṃ prakṣipet
11.7.2.3	yam uddiśya japet tasya caivam eva dhīr ekāvartaṃ dvirāvartaṃ trirāvartaṃ saptāvartaṃ yady ārogyārtham aṣṭāvartam ekatrasthe trirāvartaṃ nitye naimittike 'parimitam
11.7.2.4	yadi rudraḥ prajā abhiśāmayetottarapūrvasyāṃ diśi śatarudriyaṃ japaṃś caṅkramamāṇo japet
11.7.2.5	ekāhe japterogapāpaiḥ pramucyeta
11.7.2.6	tryahajaptena brahmahatyādipāpaiḥ kuṣṭhādibhyaḥ pramucyeta
11.7.2.7	anena vidhinā na grāme na strīsravaṇe na śrāddha āmantrito na paśusaṃnidhau na pūrvāparāṃ rātriṃ brahmacārī nāntyajadarśane na rajasvalādarśane na vyāyāmaṃ kurvīta
11.7.2.8	samāpteṣu yathākāmaṃ prārthayitvāghorebhya iti japitvā yaḥ patha iti visarjayet
11.7.2.9	tenodakena yajamānam abhiṣiñcet
11.7.2.10	apratirathaṃ japan gṛham āvartayet
11.7.2.11	brāhmaṇe yo japet sa sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt
11.7.2.12	vidhihīne viparītaṃ syād brāhmaṇasya yajamānasya ca
11.7.3.1	śucisnāto jitendriyo labdhāśīr ṛṣichandodevatāviniyogo nyāsapūrvakaṃ rudraṃ japet
11.7.3.2	aghora ṛṣī rudro devatā bṛhatī chandaḥ sarvakarmaṇi nyāse viniyoga ākhuṃ te rudra paśuṃ karomīty āntād anuvākasyeti hṛdayam idaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama ity āntād anuvākasyeti śiro brahmaṇaspata iti ṣaḍṛcaṃ brahma jajñānaṃ brahmā devānām iti śikhām apratiratham iti kavacam ādityānām avasā nūtaneneti dve ṣaḍṛcau cakṣuṣī śatarudriyam ity astram
11.7.3.3	evaṃ nyāsam āvāhanavisarjanāntam
11.7.3.4	praṇamya japaṃ nivedayet
11.7.3.5	pālāśasamidha ājyaplutās tilāhutibhir namaḥ śaṃbhave ceti tisṛbhiḥ ṣaḍdvādaśa vā juhuyāt
11.7.3.6	snānatarpaṇajapahomārcanarato yaḥ saṃvatsare japet
11.7.3.6a	sa daśāphalam āpnoti brahmaghno 'tiviśudhyati
11.7.3.6c	surāpaḥ suvarṇahartā goghno vā vṛṣalīpatiḥ
11.7.3.6e	mucyate sarvapāpebhyo rudralokaṃ sa gachati
11.7.3.7	rudrajāpīhataṃ dattam anantyāya kalpate
11.8.1.1	athātaḥ pravarādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.1.2	tad etad brāhmaṇaṃ bhavaty ārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte bandhor eva naity atho saṃtatyā iti
11.8.1.3	ekaṃ vṛṇīte dvau vṛṇīte trīnvṛṇīte na caturo vṛṇīte na pañcātipravṛṇīte vā
11.8.1.4	ihaike manuvad ity evaikārṣeyaṃ sārvavarṇikaṃ pradiśanti / kasyo hetor iti / mānavyo hi prajā iti
11.8.1.5	na devair na manuṣyair ārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīta / ṛṣibhir evārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte
11.8.1.6	yaḥ parārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte paraṃ yajñasyāśīr gached iti śrutir āvṛścyate vā eṣa oṣadhībhyaḥ paśubhyaḥ pitṛbhyo yaś ca parapravarān pravṛṇīte
11.8.1.7	tad etad anyatra brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyām itarāsāṃ prajānām uktaṃ bhavati
11.8.1.8	ita evordhvān adhvaryur vṛṇīte pūrvavad amutaś cāmuto 'rvāco hotā dvitavad āmantritavac ca
11.8.1.9	bhṛgūn evāgre vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.1.10	jāmadagnyā vātsyāḥ
11.8.1.11	ānuśātaki vaihati paila śaunakāyani jīvanti kāmbalodari vaihīnari vairohitya ḷekhyāyani vaiśāki vaiśvānara vairūpākṣi paukāśeraḷānāṃ pārṇili vṛkāśvakānā muccairmanyu sāvarṇi vālmīkiśeralānāṃ vaiṣṭapureya pālākṣi taulakeśināma samṛtabhāgārtabhāga mārkaṇḍeya maṇḍu māṇḍavya vibhāṇḍaka māṇḍūkeyārvanānāṃ sphenamadbhūtī sthaulapiṇḍi śaiṣāpatya śārkarākṣa devamatīnā māyaṇārcāyanāhvāyana gāṅgāyana vaiśampāyana vāyavyāyanauduntyāyana saurayī dārbhi mālāyana śārṅgarava gālava cāṇūkeya vaikarṇiḥ śaunakarṇiḥ śauṇḍakarṇiḥ sāṃkṛtyaitiśāyanānāṃ yājñeya bhrāṣṭreya kṣmālā aṇḍa pārimaṇḍalāyanālundhiḥ krauṣṭi saudhakīnāṃ paiṅgalāyana sātyakāyana kaucahasti kovahnaṇḍi sāṃkhyamitra cāndramitra cāndramasyānulomi kauṭilya śaunakāyani kāṃsya śāradvata maudgalyo vādyāḷehreyi nimithi śākalyoṣṭrākṣi vākāyanyanumati jaihmyāśama śokajihvātmadamani vāṭāra kirāṇi mājānāti kāśakṛtsnauṣu srucato trāna vaihīkāri śaukrāyaṇāḥ śākṛṇiḥ śākaṭāyanā goṣṭhāyanā golāyanā ḍākavyāyanā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.1.12	teṣāṃ pañcārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava cyāvanāpnavānaurva jāmadagnyeti hotā jamadagnivad ūrvavad apnavānavac cyavanavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.1.13	vaidā nimathitās teṣāṃ pañcārṣeḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava cyāvanāpnavāna vaida naimathiteti hotā nimathitavad vidavad apnavānavac cyavanavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.1.14	āvadhyāyanā mauñjāyanās teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava cyāvanāvadhyeti hotāvadhyavac cyavanavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.1	atha jamadagnīnāṃ vidāḥ
11.8.2.2	prācīnayogyāḥ pulastyā traidabhṛtāḥ krauñcāyanābhyajātās taugāyanā āvaṭāḥ śākarṇinā bhālvaśayo bhārgavā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.2.3	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava cyāvanāpnavāneti hotāpnavānavac cyavanavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.4	braudheyā mārgapathā grāmyāyaṇir atha naikasī āpastambir vibhīlli kārṇi kārdamir ārṣṭiṣeṇa gardabha śātapathi ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.2.5	teṣāṃ pañcārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava cyāvanāpnavānārṣṭiṣeṇānūpeti hotānūpavad ṛṣṭiṣeṇavad apnavānavac cyavanavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.6	āpiśāyanāḥ kāpiśāyanāḥ drauṇāyanāḥ khālāyanāḥ avicakṣā maitreyā atha iya āmodāyanā āpiśalā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.2.7	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava vādhryaśva daivodāseti hotā divodāsavad vadhryaśvavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.8	vaitahavya yāska mādhūna mauka jīvantyāyano atha bhāgaleya bhāgavijñeya kauśāmbeya vṛkāśvaki mādāhi gaurikṣita dairghyacita vāleya pāñcadhanā pauṣṇāvatā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.2.9	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava vaitahavya sāvedaseti hotā savedovad vītahavyavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.10	vatsapurodhasānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava vātsa paurodhaseti hotā purodhasavad vatsavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.11	vedaviśvajyotiṣās teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava veda viśvajyotiṣeti hotā viśvajyotiṣavad vedavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.12	pārthavainyānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / bhārgava vainya pārtheti hotā pṛthuvad venavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.2.13	gārtsamadāḥ śunakāḥ
11.8.2.14	yajñavacā saukariḥ kārdamāyanā rājabādhavyāś caukṣāś corāḥ śrotriyāḥ pratyarā śunakā ity eteṣām avivāḥ
11.8.2.15	teṣām ekārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / gārtsamadeti hotā gṛtsamadavad ity adhvaryur yadi vā dvyārṣeyo bhārgava gārtsamadeti hotā gṛtsamadavad bhṛguvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.3.1	aṅgiraso vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.3.2	aucathyā gautamāḥ
11.8.3.3	tauḍeyā abhijita voghāya naikākṣa rāhugaṇyāḥ kṣairakaṭaikastamarāṇāṃ kairāti sāralopānāṃ karoti kāśapārīṇāṃ pauṣpiṇḍa bhāgala vaḍauḍavānām upabindu mānthareṣāṇāṃ rauhiṇāyanā amalakā krolayimāḥ krauṃcāḥ kroṣṭā āruṇayaḥ pārthivā saudāmini kācākṣa kauralyā akṣa apādapakṣa vāsamūli vaṃśamulmiṃ śapitṛ vāsapuṣpiḥ sauṣya saukṣmāyaṇa kauḍalyā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.3.4	teṣāṃ pañcārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasaucathya gautamauśija kākṣīvateti hotā kakṣīvadvad uśijavad gotamavad ucathyavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.3.5	āyāsyānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasāyāsya gautameti hotā gotamavad ayāsyavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.3.6	athātreyāyaṇi mādhūkarṇi vālkali saupiṣṭyāgniveśyānāṃ śālāthala vārāha śauṅga kṛpaṇaparṇa prāvāhaṇeyānāṃ māślāya vyāyogichaṃdāta khārigrīvīṇām aiṣumati śādya kāvakikāvikāyanānāṃ naitundi lira vaidhaṃkīnāṃ vaidhakīkayā carātaki manahālānāṃ sauvastambi taulvali pauṣuyāvaddiśīnāṃ śāla vāḷauha devamata harikarṇa drāṅgava cauceya kaumudagandhi khāriṇādi rājastambi sāmastambi somastambi audameghi gāṇḍaki lauhitaki kāṇḍaka dhānā kulaka sātyamugri śaivayatha bhāradvāja ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.3.7	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa bārhaspatya bhāradvājeti hotā bharadvājavad bṛhaspativad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.3.8	kāṇāyaṇāḥ kaivalayo 'tha vatsatarāyaṇāḥ krauṇḍāyanā vārddhanayo 'tho vāṃśāyanāś ca ye bhrāṣṭrakṛdbhrāṣṭrabinduś caindrāli sāyakāyanaḥ kolī ca krīkā nīsāṃtvakṛtsnāpurāvaṭa lāvaki bhālūvirupamarkaṭi protsaṅgiḥ śyāmāyana paiṅgalāyana sāṃbharabhāmat ... ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.3.9	teṣāṃ pañcārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa bārhaspatya bhāradvāja śainya gārgyeti hotā gargavacchinivad bharadvājavad bṛhaspativad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.3.10	tetirari kavibhūmo gargā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.3.11	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa śainya gārgyeti hotā gargavacchinivad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.1	kapistaraḥ svastitaro bindur daṇḍiḥ śaktiḥ patañjalir bhojava jrarudhuś caivadviśālī śītakiḥ addhaṃ rājakeśo cauccuṭī śāṃśāpi kalaśīkaṇṭhaḥ kārīrayo vānyāyanā vāmadhyāyanāḥ kāpyāḥ kavaya ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.2	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasāmahīyaurukṣayeti hotorukṣayavad amahīyavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.3	saṃkṛti pautimāṣi taṇḍi śambhuḥ śevapāyanānāṃ jānaki tenailvakādvyalātavyārṣabhi lāṃgaṃdhi cārāyaṇī ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.4	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa sāṃkṛtya gaurivīteti hotā gaurivītivat saṃkṛtivad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.5	haritaḥ kautsa śaṅkha darbha paiṅga bhaimagava mādrakāri gāṇakāri hāstidāsi lāveraṇi kālaśīte ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.6	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasāmbarīṣa yauvanāśveti hotā yuvanāśvavad ambarīṣavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.7	ruruṃgākyāyanā ḍaśca tṛtīyaḥ śākaṭāyanaḥ caturtho gardabho nārī tataḥ prākāra sauvāra markaṭo ramaṇaḥ śaṇaḥ kaṇvā mārkaṭayo rāmaṇeyāḥ śāṇāyanā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.8	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasājamīḍha kāṇveti hotā kaṇvavad ajamīḍhavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.9	atha vaiṣṇuvṛddhi śaṭhamarṣaṇa chatṛṇa potṛṇa gotṛṇa bādarāyaṇā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.10	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa paurukutsa trāsadasyaveti hotā trasadasyuvat purukutsavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.11	rathītarāṇāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa vairūpa pārṣadaśveti hotā pṛṣadaśvavad virūpavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.12	raṣābhagānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa vāmadevya gautameti hotā gotamavad vāmadevavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.13	hiraṇyagarbha chatrakayo mudgalā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.14	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavatyāṅgirasa bhārmyaśva maudgalyeti hotā mudgalavad bhṛmyaśvavad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.15	ṛkṣabharadvājānāṃ pañcārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa bārhaspatya bhāradvāja vāndana mātavacaseti hotā matavacovad vandavad bharadvājavad bṛhaspativad aṅgirovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.4.16	atha yāny etāni dvyāmuṣyāyaṇāni kulāni bhavanti yathaitac chauṅgaśaiśirayor bharadvājāḥ śauṅgāḥ katāḥ śaiśiraya ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.4.17	teṣāṃ pañcārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āṅgirasa bārhaspatya bhāradvāja śauṅga śaiśireti hotā śiśiravac chuṅgavad bharadvājavad bṛhaspativad aṅgarovad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.1	viśvāmitrān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.5.2	vaiśvāmitrā devarātāś caikita gālava vāratantavāḥ kuśikā vātaṇḍaś ca śalaṅkā āśvāvatāyanāḥ śyāmāyanā yājñavalkyā jāvālāḥ saindhavāyanā bābhravyā yaś ca varṣīya sāsityā atha sauśrutā audheprāḥ saurathāyaḥ kājāliyājaya ārjunākṣi pāryodari sumantu jaimini kharavākhali ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.3	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra daivarātaudaleti hotodalavad devarātavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.4	devaśravasā devatarasā śraumata kāmakāyanā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.5	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra daivaśravasa daivataraseti hotā devatarovad devaśravovad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.6	trīṇy etāni raiṇavāni kulāni bhavanti kathyakā śvodūraṇa śvodūhayaś cety eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.7	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra kāthaka kāthyaketi hotā kathyakavat kāthavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.8	atha kamandaka dhanaṃjaya piḷakaṭa pārthiva bandhala pāṇinānām ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.9	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra mādhuchandasāghamarṣaṇeti hotāghamarṣaṇavan madhuchandovad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.10	ajā mādhuchandasā mārgamitrā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.11	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra mādhuchandasājyoti hotājavan madhuchandovad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.12	āśmarathyāḥ kāmalāyatino bandhula kauśiketihotā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.13	teṣāṃ dvyārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitrāṣṭaketi hotāṣṭakavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.14	pūraṇā vāridhāpayantā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.15	teṣāṃ dvyārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra pauraṇeti hotā pūraṇavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.16	gāthino raiṇavāsteṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra gāthina raiṇaveti hotā reṇuvad gāthivad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.17	hiraṇyaretasānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra hiraṇya retaseti hotā retasavad dhiraṇyavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.18	suvarṇaretasānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra sauvarṇa retaseti hotā retasavat suvarṇavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.19	kapotaretasānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra kāpota retaseti hotā retasavat kapotavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.20	ghṛtakauśikānāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra ghārta kauśiketi hotā kuśikavad ghṛtavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.21	śāṭharamāṭharāṇāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra śāṭhara māṭhareti hotā maṭharavac chaṭharavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.22	atha sāhula māhula uhala kohala jaṃvila śāvila śātila phāhula yāmila yādadhi śādadhi ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.23	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra sāhula māhuleti hotā māhulavat sāhulavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.5.24	athodumbarāyaṇiḥ śaiśira taikāyanti tārukṣyāyaṇi velāyana vedāyana maudāyana caudāyana gaṅgāyana kātyāyana kātyātkīla kārī lācakīty eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.5.25	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vaiśvāmitra kātyātkīleti hotātkīlavat katavad viśvāmitravad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.6.1	vasiṣṭhān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.6.2	vasiṣṭhānām ekārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati ye 'nya upamanyuparāśarebhyaḥ kuṇḍinebhyaś ca
11.8.6.3	vaidyāghrapadyā aupagavā vaigrayaḥ sāsāmalāyanāḥ kapiṣṭhalā auḍulomāśvalāyanā vaiṭārakā gopāyanā baudhāyanāś cūḍākavyāyanā atha vāhyākī jātūkarṇyā haritayo 'tho vākurayaś ca ye āyaḥsthūṇāḥ śucivṛkṣā laumāyanya bahyavādi bahmakṛdeya bahmavideya bahmavileyaḥ svastikaraḥ kāṇṭheviddhi maṇḍi cauli caulikā kālohalī saumanasāyaṇirāvaṇi cauli gauriśravasārjunākṣā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.6.4	teṣām ekārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vāsiṣṭheti hotā vasiṣṭhavad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.6.5	upamanyūn vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.6.6	śailālayo mahākarṇāḥ kauravyā atha traivarṇāḥ kapiñjalā dāvalaśikhī bhāgavittāyanāś ca ye ḍokavyāyanā oṃpālakhī vāvālkalayaḥ śāntātapāḥ kārḍurirākatmāveyā atho lavayaś ca ye yortha atha sachāgyāyana ālavyāyanā kaumārāyaṇāḥ kaulodakiraudgāhamānayaḥ evākari lākṣmaṇeyāḥ gāṇḍūlavoddhaki sāṃkhyāyanā aupamanyavāḥ kauṇḍodari kaidarbhi nāhaki bāhavi dhaumāvata mauñjāyana śaśakāyanā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.6.7	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vāsiṣṭhābharadvasavaindrapramadeti hotendrapramadavad ābharadvasuvad vasiṣṭhavad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.6.8a	prārohayo vaikalayaḥ plākṣayaḥ kaumudādayaḥ
11.8.6.8c	hāryaśvir eṣāṃ pañcama ete raktāḥ parāśarāḥ
11.8.6.8a	kāṇḍūśayo vāhatayā jāṃjayo maimanāyanāḥ
11.8.6.8c	gopālireṣāṃ pañcama ete nīlāḥ parāśarāḥ
11.8.6.8a	kārṣṇājināḥ kapiśroḍhāḥ kārkayaḥ śāntātapāḥ
11.8.6.8c	puṣkarasādireṣāṃ pañcama ete kṛṣṇāḥ parāśarāḥ
11.8.6.8a	āviṣṭāyanā vārṣṇāyanā śmāmeya lokāyaś ca
11.8.6.8c	vaikṣireṣāṃ pañcama ete gaurāḥ parāśarāḥ
11.8.6.8a	khāllāyanā vārṣāyaṇi pūrṇayo bilvayūpayaḥ
11.8.6.8c	nārṇireṣāṃ pañcama ete śuklāḥ parāśarāḥ
11.8.6.8	ete triṃśatparāśarā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.6.9	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vāsiṣṭha śāktya pārāśaryeti hotā parāśaravac chaktivad vasiṣṭhavad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.6.10	aupasvastiḥ svastayaś cālohāyanāś ca ye mādhyaṃdinā ākṣitayaḥ paippalādi divaṃkarṣī kuṇḍino mitrāvaruṇā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.6.11	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / vāsiṣṭha kauṇḍinya maitrāvaruṇeti hotā mitrāvaruṇavat kuṇḍinavad vasiṣṭhavad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.7.1	kaśyapān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.7.2	āgrāyaṇāś cāgrāyaṇā graivāyaṇā vṛṣagaṇā somabhūtā śonavyā mauṣakiritikāyanā audavrajirmāṭharaś ca kaijāli atha lākṣmaṇayo vaidhakayaḥ ślokatyā yaś ca bhaumani devatayā gomeyādā athotthāsvayaṃsvāpa dhūmrāyaṇāḥ subabhruś cāthorṣyāyaṇā kārṣyāyaṇā svāroyaṇā ḍākavāyaṇāḥ śatrubhayo bhiryogādiḥ śarakāḥ kāṣṭāyaṇāḥ śākādaḥ śālihotrāś cāyamājānanāthāḥ kuvamimāḥ cakridāḥ dākṣapāṇayo mārīcayo māṣaśarāvir agniśarmāyaṇaś ca ye hāstidāsi yailmailitānyakṛti kauṣītakī saumiśrī kāṇḍā vāyani vāruṇi vaivarī śaivarayo jighāna hastikāśyapa paiṭhīnasa kaikaseya pratiṣeya sauśyavasamoya saryāgnā vasamopa dārbhaḥ pālaśāyinaḥ kaduka bhaikṣi ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.7.3	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / kāśyapāvatsāra naidhruveti hotā nidhruvavad avatsāravat kaśyapavad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.7.4	ānaṣṭayo bhāgurayaḥ śyenapo 'thājāpālayaḥ śairī ṣiraudavāhī ca śairaṃdhri aupaśavīyaḥ saumyakṛkoyuṣī kālāśi laukkākṣa idaṃdha ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.7.5	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / kāśyapāvatsāra vāsiṣṭheti hotā vasiṣṭhavad avatsāravat kaśyapavad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.7.6	sáṃbhujā jalibhraśvobhau bhūpapurodha jalaṃdhara mujo mayūraḥ paryagoṣṭho gardabhīmukho hiraṇyavāhur ādityavarṇaḥ saudāmilubho śauśila gobhilo kuhalo vṛkakhaṇḍaś cety ete gukuraṇṭayaḥ uttaraḥ śāntiketuś cety ete devajātayaḥ vedāyana jāṅgharāyaṇa śatrūhāyana audameghāstṛṇavasta śaṇḍilo mahākā bhallakaś ca vāyukīstārkalistetṛcodvudi sauṣmiṇeyā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.7.7	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavati / kāśyapāsita daivaleti hotā śāṇḍilāsita daivaleti vā devalavad asitavat kaśyapavad ity adhvaryur devalavad asitavac chaṇḍilavad iti vā
11.8.8.1	atrīn vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.8.2	kārmaryāyāṇi śaṃkilayaṃścādyo śākhārathayaś ca ye āghrāyaṇā vāmarathyā gopavanās tārṇabindava auddālakī śaunakarṇyatho vālūtapayaś ca ye gauragrīviḥ kairandiś ca caitrāyaṇāś ca ye nākarṣyayaṃti pauriṃdyatho vatsāthapāś ca ye gali chāgali bhāgali vāhudantyendreya dauchāyātreyaḥ sauddhūtakī varṣāṇaki kṛṣṇa chandogīty eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.8.3	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty ātreyārcanānasa śyāvāśveti hotā śyāvāśvavad arcanānasavad atrivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.8.4	plākṣirdākṣirvyāliḥ paurṇaviraurṇavāpi śilaṃvino mauñjakeśī bhalandano baijavāpi śirīṣaś ca maiyaṇyo dūtiḥ saupuṣpiḥ sāmapuṣpiḥ somapuṣpiḥ hiraṇyapuṣpiścandrikardraki kākaśīrpi kākālaśīty eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.8.5	tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty ātreya gāviṣṭhira paurvātitheti hotā pūrvātithivad gaviṣṭhiravad atrivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.8.6	putrikāputrān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.8.7	hāleyā vāleyā daubheyā śaubhreyā kaubhreyā vāmarathya gopavana viṣṭira putrikāputrā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.8.8	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavatyātreya gāviṣṭhira pautriketi hotā putrikāvad gaviṣṭhiravad atrivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.9.1	agastīn vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.9.2	kukūla upaka balakā lāṃvakāyana śālaṃkāyana dhāriṇi dhauraṇī saudhanvā saukṛtya kalmāṣadaṇḍirapauturauturāyaṇānāṃ śaurbhyāṃyanā govyādhilā śilādya śaivapathārbudānām aidilamā evayāyadūtā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.9.3	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āgastya dārḍhacyutaidhmavāheti hotedhmavāhavad dṛḍhacyutavad agastivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.9.4	akra śakra śukra jātye haimaudakīty eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.9.5	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āgastya māhendra māyobhuveti hotā mayobhuvavan mahendravad agstivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.9.6	prācīnapravaṇāḥ kāyeyāḥ akra śukra śuddha haṃsa cāṣa bhāṣa haimavarca himodakāḥ ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.9.7	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āgastya haimavarca haimodaketi hotā himodakavad dhimavarcavad agastivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.9.8	akri cakri arci carci himodaki pāriṇakā ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.9.9	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āgastya pināyaka pāriṇaketi hotā pāriṇakavat pināyakavad agastivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.9.10	naṃdi vimali dhimali mimītaki pināyaki sāyaki ity eteṣām avivāhaḥ
11.8.9.11	teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āgastya pināyaka sāyaketi hotā sāyakavat pināyakavad agastivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.9.12	madhyamapūraṇās teṣāṃ tryārṣeyaḥ pravaro bhavaty āgastya mādhyama pauraṇeti hotā puraṇavan madhyamavad agastivad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.10.1	vyākhyātāḥ pravarāḥ / vaikṛtāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.10.2	atha dvitayyo brāhmaṇānāṃ samutpattayo bhavanti / teṣāṃ samutpattiṃ pratipattiṃ ca vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.8.10.3	yeṣāṃ puruṣataḥ prajotpattir avichinnā bhavati te saṃhitakulīnāḥ
11.8.10.4	ye sapta bhūyaḥ pañcapuruṣaṃ vā yoniśrutivṛttaśīlasaṃpannā ṛtavatām ṛtavantas te pitṛmantaḥ paitṛmatyārṣeyā bhavanty ārtvijīnām
11.8.10.5	atha dattakakrītakakṛtimaputrikāputrāḥ paraparigraheṇa nānārṣeyā ye jātā dvyāmuṣyāyaṇā bhavanti yathaitac chauṅgaśaiśirīṇāṃ bharadvājaudamedhīnāṃ laukākṣīnāṃ ca yāni cānyāny evaṃ samutpattīni kulāni bhavanti
11.8.10.6	teṣāṃ tathaiva pravarāḥ syur dvipravarasaṃnipāte pūrvaḥ pravara utpādayitur uttaraḥ parigrahītuḥ
11.8.10.7	api vā trayo 'nye trayo 'nye / tan na tathā kuryāt tasmāt trīn eva pañca vā pravṛṇīte
11.8.10.8	atha yadi pitṛvyeṇa jñātinaikārṣeyeṇa ye jātāḥ saṃhitakulīnāḥ teṣāṃ parigrahītur eva bhavati
11.8.10.9	atha yady eṣāṃ svāsu bhāryāsv apatyaṃ na syād rikthaṃ hareyuḥ piṇḍaṃ caibhyas tripuruṣaṃ dadyur yadi syād ubhābhyām eva dadyur ity ācāryavacanam
11.8.10.10	dve kuryād ekaśrāddhe kuryād vā pṛthag anudiśyaikapiṇḍe dvāv anukīrtayet parigrahītāraṃ cotpādayitāraṃ cā tṛtīyāt puruṣāt
11.8.10.11	ārṣeyasyāparijñānād eteṣām eva pravarāṇām ādyaṃ pravaraṃ pravṛṇīte / paripraśnena vā yaṃ yasyopapannaṃ manyeta taṃ tasya kuryāt
11.8.10.12	purohitapravaro vā syād ācāryapravaro vā rājanya etenaiva tu pravareṇa vaiśyapravaro vyākhyātaḥ
11.8.10.13	yadi sārṣṭiṃ pravṛṇīte mānavaiḍa paurūravaseti hotā purūravovad iḍāvan manuvad ity adhvaryuḥ
11.8.10.14	sārṣṭiṃ pravṛṇīyuḥ ...
11.8.10.15	purohitapravarāv eva rājanyavaiśyau syātām
11.8.10.16	dhanaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam ṛṣīṇāṃ kīrtanaṃ śubham
11.8.10.17	divyaṃ varṣasahasram ekaikasyarṣer ātithyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavati yaḥ pravarādhyāyam adhīte
11.8.10.18	maithunagotrālābha ṛṣyantarāṇām avirodhīti
11.8.10.19	eṣa mahāñ śakuniḥ samāpto vedānāṃ mūlaṃ dharmasya cāgraṃ rudraiḥ samadhikaṃ vṛddhaṃ vṛddhaiḥ
11.8.10.20	nāputrāya nāśiṣyāya nāsaṃvatsaroṣitāya dadyāt
11.8.10.21	sarveṣāṃ paṅktipāvanānām upariṣṭād bhavati yaḥ pravarādhyāyam adhīte yaḥ pravarādhyāyam adhīta iti
11.9.1.1	athātaḥ śrāddhakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.9.1.2	agnim upasamādhāya nirmanthya cāsagotrān ayugmān apradakṣiṇam āmantrya brāhmaṇān pūrvedyur ye mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaś ca daśapuruṣaṃ samanusthitā vidyātapobhyāṃ kalyāṇakarmaṇaḥ śucayaḥ śuklavāsaso 'parāhṇe prācīnāvavītikṛtamaṇḍaloparipacchaucān ācāntān prāṅmukhān pitṝn udaṅmukhān viśvedevān bhojayet
11.9.1.3	arghyapātrāṇy upakalpayed dvau daive trīn pitrya ekaikam ubhayatra vā
11.9.1.4	sam anyā yantīty apa āsicya sumanasaś cotpūya yavān prakṣipya viśvān devān āvāhayiṣyāmīty uktvā brāhmaṇair anujñāto viśve devā ṛtāvṛdho viśve devāso asridha iti yavān pradakṣiṇaṃ prakiret
11.9.1.5	pavitre pāṇau pradāya hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucaya ity uktvā viśve devā eṣa vo arghyaḥ // pitṝn pitāmahān prapitāmahān āvāhayiṣyāmīty uktvā brahmaṇair anujñāta uśantas tvā havāmahe paretana pitaraḥ somyāsa iti tilān pradakṣiṇaṃ prakiret
11.9.1.6	pavitre pāṇu pradāya nāmagotre samuccārya mama pitar eṣa te 'rghyaḥ pitāmaha prapitāmeti / gandhapuṣpadhūpadīpāchādanāntair arcayitvā ghṛtāktam annam ādāya mekṣaṇapāṇir agnau karaṇaṃ kariṣyāmīty uktvā brāhmaṇair anujñātaḥ somāya pitṛmate svadhā nama iti juhoti
11.9.1.7	yamāyāṅgirasvate pitṛmate svadhā nama iti dvitīyām agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā nama ity asaṃsaktān dakṣiṇārdhapūrvārdhe tṛtīyāṃ hutvocchiṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradāya śeṣaṃ piṇḍapitṛyajñavan nidadhyāt
11.9.2.1a	api naḥ svakule bhūyād yo no dadyāt trayodaśīm
11.9.2.1c	pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca
11.9.2.2a	sauvarṇeṣu ca pātreṣu rājataudumbareṣu ca
11.9.2.2c	dattam akṣayyatāṃ yāti khaḍgenāryakṛtena ca
11.9.2.3	payaḥ pṛthivyām iti pāyasaṃ dadyān madhu vātā ṛtāyata iti madhv āyurdeti ghṛtaṃ dadyāt
11.9.2.4	satyaṃ tvartena pariṣiñcāmīti pariṣicya tūṣṇīṃ vā pṛthivī te pātram iti pātrābhimantraṇam
11.9.2.5	brāhmaṇāṅguṣṭham ādāya viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣasveti viśvedevān viṣṇo kavyaṃ rakṣasveti pitṝn udakaṃ pāṇau pradāya oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti trir uktvā madhu vātā ṛtāyata iti tryṛcaṃ prīyantāṃ pitaraḥ prīyantāṃ pitāmahāḥ prīyantāṃ prapitāmahā iti vāgyatas tṛpyantv itīṣṭatamāny annāni dadyāt
11.9.2.6	triḥ sāvitrīm adhīte trīṃś cādito 'nuvākān
11.9.2.7	atra pitaro mādayadhvaṃ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvāṃho 'vayajyośantas tvā havāmahe 'tra pitaro mādayadhvam ity uktvā parāyanti
11.9.2.8	kṛṇuṣva pājā iti pañca sa te jānāty ā no agne punantu mā pitara iti pitṝn aśnatsu japet
11.9.2.9	tṛptāḥ stha iti pṛchet tṛptāḥ sma iti pratyāhuḥ
11.9.2.10	sakṛdācānteṣv agnidagdhā iti bhūmau vikiraṃ ninayet
11.9.2.11a	agnidagdhās tu ye jīvā ye 'py adagdhāḥ kule mama
11.9.2.11c	bhūmau dattena toyena tṛptā yāntu parāṃ gatim
11.9.2.11	ity udakaṃ ninīya piṇḍapitṛyajñavat piṇḍān nidadhyāt
11.9.2.12	athāgrabhūmim āsicya suprokṣitam astv ity akṣayyam uttiṣṭhety upotthāpya vājevāja ity abhipravrajyā mā vājasyeti pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryād rajataṃ dadyāt pūrṇapātraṃ vā
11.9.2.13a	daśa pūrvān daśāparān ātmānaṃ caikaviṃśakam
11.9.2.13c	śrāddhakṛn mocayet pāpān mahato 'py enasaḥ pitṝn
11.9.2.14a	śrāddhaṃ ca yo na dadyāt pitṛbhyaś ca kadācana
11.9.2.14c	ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ
11.9.2.15a	yad eva tarpayaty adbhiḥ pitṝñ śrāddhe samāhitaḥ
11.9.2.15c	tenaiva sarvam āpnoti pitṛyajñakriyāphalam
11.9.2.15	pitṛyajñakriyāphalam iti
11.9.3.1	atha vṛddhiśrāddhakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
11.9.3.2a	atha cābhyudaye prāpte devatāsthāpanaṃ smṛtam
11.9.3.2c	jātidharmakulāmnātaṃ lokānāṃ vṛddhikāraṇam
11.9.3.3a	karmādiṣu ca sarveṣu mātaraḥ sagaṇādhipāḥ
11.9.3.3c	pūjanīyāḥ prayatnena pūjitāḥ pūjayanti tāḥ
11.9.3.4a	brahmāṇyādyāḥ smṛtāḥ sapta durgākṣetrādhipas tathā
11.9.3.4c	vṛddhauvṛddhau sadā pūjyāḥ paścān nāndīmukhān pitṝn
11.9.3.5a	tisraḥ pūjyāḥ pituḥ pakṣe tisro mātāmahe tathā
11.9.3.5c	ity etā mātaraḥ proktā pitṛmātṛṣvasāṣṭamī
11.9.3.6a	pratimāsu ca śrubhrāsu likhitvā vā paṭādiṣu
11.9.3.6c	api vākṣatapuñjeṣu naivedyaiś ca pṛthakpṛthak
11.9.3.6a	kuḍyalagnāṃ vasordhārāṃ ghṛtenaiva tu kārayet
11.9.3.6c	kārayet sapta vā pañca nātinīcāṃ ca nocchritām
11.9.3.7a	āyuṣyāṇi ca śāntyarthaṃ japetatra samāhitaḥ
11.9.3.7c	māṅgalyair gītavāditrair mātṝṇāṃ pūjanaṃ smṛtam
11.9.3.8a	asakṛd yāni karmāṇi kriyeran karmakāribhiḥ
11.9.3.8c	pratiprayogaṃ naitāḥ syur mātaraḥ śrāddham eva ca
11.9.3.9a	sakṛd eva bhavec chrāddhaṃ homamantrāḥ pṛthakpṛthak
11.9.3.10a	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi viśeṣa iha yo bhavet
11.9.3.11a	prātarāmantritān viprān yugmān ubhayatas tathā
11.9.3.11c	upaveśya kuśān dadyād ṛjunaiva hi pāṇinā
11.9.3.12a	haritā yajñiyā darbhāḥ pītakāḥ pākayajñikāḥ
11.9.3.12c	samūlāḥ pitṛdaivatyāḥ kalmāṣā vaiśvadevikāḥ
11.9.3.12e	dvādaśāṅgulapramāṇena pitṛtīrthena saṃskṛtāḥ
11.9.3.13a	sadā paricared bhaktyā pitṝn apy atra devavat
11.9.3.14a	pitṛbhya iti datteṣu upaveśya kuśeṣu tān
11.9.3.14c	gotranāmāni varjanti pitṛbhyo 'rghyaṃ pradāpayet
11.9.3.15a	nātrāpasavyakaraṇaṃ na pitryaṃ tīrtham iṣyate
11.9.3.15c	pātrāṇāṃ pūraṇādīni devatīrthena kārayet
11.9.3.16a	jyeṣṭhottarakarān yugmān karāgrāgrapavitrakān
11.9.3.16c	kṛtvārghyaṃ saṃpradātavyaṃ naikaikasyātra dīyate
11.9.3.17a	madhu madhv iti yas tatra trir japo 'śitum ichatām
11.9.3.17c	gāyatryanantaraṃ so 'tra madhumantratrivarjitaḥ
11.9.3.18a	anya eva japaḥ kāryo rākṣoghnaḥ suradevavat
11.9.3.19a	saṃpannam iti tṛptāḥ stha praśnasthāne vidhīyate
11.9.3.19c	susaṃpannam iti prokte śeṣam annaṃ nivedayet
11.9.3.20a	brūyāt tṛpteṣu saṃpannam iti tṛptāḥ stha pārvaṇe
11.9.3.20c	vikiraṃ ca tathā dadyāj juhuyāc ca ṛcāṃ vinā
11.9.3.21a	asomapāś ca ye devā yajñabhāgabahiṣkṛtāḥ
11.9.3.21c	teṣām annaṃ pradātavyaṃ vikiraṃ vaiśvadevikam
11.9.3.22	navāvarān bhojayed yugmān vṛddhiṣu pradakṣiṇam upacāro yavais tilārthān kurvanti
11.9.3.23	dadhyakṣatabadaramiśrān piṇḍan nidadhyāt
11.9.3.24	nāndīmukhān pitṝn prīṇanti
11.9.3.25a	nāndīmukhāḥ pitara iti kuryād āvāhanādikam
11.9.3.25c	prīyantām iti ca brūyuḥ piṇḍān svāheti nikṣipet
11.9.3.26a	mātṛpūrvān pitṝn pūjya tato mātāmahāṃs tathā
11.9.3.26c	mātāmahīs tathā kecid yugmāṃś ca bhojayed dvijān
11.9.3.27a	dvaudvāv abhyudaye piṇḍāv ekaikasya pituḥpituḥ
11.9.3.27c	pārvaṇe piṇḍam ekaikaṃ trayāṇāṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak
11.9.3.28a	trayāṇām udakaṃ kāryaṃ triṣu piṇḍaḥ pravartate
11.9.3.28c	ūrdhvaṃ nāndīmukhaṃ proktaṃ nāmagotrāpaharakam
11.9.3.29a	svapitṛbhyaḥ pitā dadyāt sutasaṃskārakarmasu
11.9.3.29c	vivāhādau svapitṛbhyaḥ putro dadyāt sadaiva hi
11.9.3.30a	nāniṣṭvā tu pitṝñ śrāddhe vaidikaṃ karma ārabhet
11.9.3.30c	tebhyo 'pi pūrvedyuḥ pūrvaṃ paścān nāndīmukhān pitṝn
11.9.3.31a	ādhāne homayoś caiva vaiśvadeve tathaiva ca
11.9.3.31c	balikarmaṇi darśe ca paurṇamāse tathaiva ca
11.9.3.31a	āgrāyaṇyāṃ pākayajñe vadanty evaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ
11.9.3.31c	ekam eva bhavec chrāddham eteṣu na pṛthakpṛthak
11.9.3.32	athāgrabhūmim āsicya suprokṣitam astv iti śivā āpaḥ santv iti yugmān evodakena ca saumanasyam astv iti ca puṣpam akṣataṃ cāriṣṭaṃ cāstv ity akṣatān pratipādayet
11.9.3.33a	akṣayodakadānaṃ ca tv arghyadānavad iṣyate
11.9.3.33c	ṣaṣṭhyaiva nityaṃ tat kuryān na caturthyā kadācana
11.9.3.34a	prāthanāsu pratiprokte sarvāsv eva dvijottamaiḥ
11.9.3.34c	yugmān eva svastivācya aṅguṣṭhāgragrahaṃ sadā
11.9.3.34e	kṛtvā dhuryasya viprasya praṇamyānuvrajet tataḥ
11.9.4.1	atha pariśiṣṭam
11.9.4.2	saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatis tasya yad udagayanaṃ śuklo 'haḥ pūrvāhṇas tad devānāṃ madhyaṃdino manuṣyāṇām aparāhṇas tat pitṝṇām atha yathobhayata ijyate
11.9.4.3a	kuryād aharahaḥ śrāddham annādyenodakena vā
11.9.4.3c	payomūlaphalair vāpi pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āharet
11.9.4.4a	aṣṭakāpārvaṇaśrāddhaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣo 'yanadvayam
11.9.4.4c	dravyabrāhmaṇasaṃpattiḥ śrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
11.9.4.5a	udvāhe putrajanane pitryeṣṭyāṃ saumike makhe
11.9.4.5c	tīrthe brāhmaṇa āyāte ṣaḍ ete jīvataḥ pituḥ
11.9.4.6a	anvaṣṭakyaṃ gayāpraptau satyāṃ yac ca mṛte 'hani
11.9.4.6c	matuḥ śrāddhaṃ sutaḥ kuryāt pitary api ca jīvati
11.9.4.7a	kanyāgate savitari yāny ahāni ca ṣoḍaśa
11.9.4.7c	kratubhis tāni tulyāni / pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam
11.9.4.8	pañcamīprabhṛtyaparapakṣasya / pañcamīṃ putrakāmaḥ ṣaṣṭhīṃ dhanakāmaḥ saptamīṃ paśukāmo 'ṣṭamīm ārogyakāmo navamīṃ tejaskāmo daśamīm annādyakāma ekādaśīm ṛddhikāmo dvādaśīṃ vṛddhikāmas trayodaśīṃ yaśaskāmaś caturdásīṃ śastrahatasyārogyakāmo 'māvāsyāyāṃ sarvakāmaḥ
11.9.4.9	tilaiḥ śrāddhaṃ puṣṭikāmaḥ kuryād apūpair ṛddhikāmo ghṛtaguḍatilais tejaskāmaḥ svastikāmaḥ saubhāgyakāma ārogyakāmo vā paramānnakṛsarānnamāṣadadhiyavāgūbhiḥ sarvakāmaḥ
11.9.4.10a	pūrvedyur āmantritair vipraiḥ pitaraḥ saṃviśanti vai
11.9.4.10c	yajamānaś ca tāṃ rātriṃ vaseyur brahmacāriṇaḥ
11.9.4.11a	śrāddhaṃ dattvā ca bhuktvā ca adhvānaṃ yo 'dhigachati
11.9.4.11c	taṃ māsaṃ tasya pitaro bhuñjate pāṃśubhojanāḥ
11.9.4.12a	śrāddhaṃ dattvā ca bhuktvā ca maithunaṃ yo 'dhigachati
11.9.4.12c	taṃ māsaṃ tasya pitaro bhuñjate retabhojanāḥ
11.9.4.13a	śrāddham adhvā bhaved aśvaḥ punar bhuṅkte tu vāyasaḥ
11.9.4.13c	karmakṛj jāyate dāsaḥ strīgamyo grāmaśūkaraḥ
11.9.4.14a	dvau daive trīn pitrya ekaikam ubhayatra vā
11.9.4.14c	bhojayet susamṛddho 'pi na prasajjeti vistaram
11.9.4.15a	satkriyāṃ deśakālau ca dravyaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpadaḥ
11.9.4.15c	pañcaitān vistaro hanti tasyānnehatu vistaram
11.9.4.16a	yatnena bhojayec chrāddhe bahvṛcaṃ vedapāragam
11.9.4.16c	śākhāntagam athādhvaryuṃ chandogaṃ vā samāptigam
11.9.4.17a	pañcāgnis trisuparṇaś ca triṇāciketaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit
11.9.4.17c	brahmadeyānusaṃtāno jyeṣṭhasāmaga eva ca
11.9.4.18a	mātāmahaṃ mātulaṃ ca svasrīyaṃ śvaśraṃ gurum
11.9.4.18c	dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ bandhum ṛtvigyājyau ca bhojayet
11.9.4.19a	yasya śrāddhe na bhuñjanti brahmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
11.9.4.19c	akṛtaṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati
11.9.4.20a	yasya śrāddhe na bhuñjante brāhmaṇāḥ svaśākhinaḥ
11.9.4.20c	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati
11.9.4.21a	vedārthavit pravaktā ca brahmacārī sadā sthitaḥ
11.9.4.21c	śatāyuś caiva vijñeyā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ
11.9.4.22a	eṣām anyatamo yasya bhuñjīta śrāddham arcitaḥ
11.9.4.22c	pitṝṇāṃ tasya tṛptiḥ syācchāśvatī sāptapauruṣī
11.9.4.23a	tilā rakṣantu daiteyān darbhā rakṣantu rākṣasān
11.9.4.23c	tasmād dāneṣu dātavyās ātmano bhūtim ichatā
